Vālmīki Rāmāyaṇa  Bālakāṇḍa
a tapaḥsvādhyāyanirataṃ tapasvī vāgvidāṃ varam
c nāradaṃ paripapraccha vālmīkir munipuṃgavam
a ko nv asmin sāmprataṃ loke guṇavān kaś ca vīryavān
c dharmajñaś ca kṛtajñaś ca satyavākyo dṛḍhavrataḥ
a cāritreṇa ca ko yuktaḥ sarvabhūteṣu ko hitaḥ
c vidvān kaḥ kaḥ samarthaś ca kaś caikapriyadarśanaḥ
a ātmavān ko jitakrodho matimān ko 'nasūyakaḥ
c kasya bibhyati devāś ca jātaroṣasya saṃyuge
a etad icchāmy ahaṃ śrotuṃ paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hi me
c maharṣe tvaṃ samartho 'si jñātum evaṃvidhaṃ naram
a śrutvā caitat trilokajño vālmīker nārado vacaḥ
c śrūyatām iti cāmantrya prahṛṣṭo vākyam abravīt
a bahavo durlabhāś caiva ye tvayā kīrtitā guṇāḥ
c mune vakṣyāmy ahaṃ buddhvā tair yuktaḥ śrūyatāṃ naraḥ
a ikṣvākuvaṃśaprabhavo rāmo nāma janaiḥ śrutaḥ
c niyatātmā mahāvīryo dyutimān dhṛtimān vaśī
a buddhimān nītimān vāgmī śrīmāñ śatrunibarhaṇaḥ
c vipulāṃso mahābāhuḥ kambugrīvo mahāhanuḥ
a mahorasko maheṣvāso gūḍhajatrur ariṃdamaḥ
c ājānubāhuḥ suśirāḥ sulalāṭaḥ suvikramaḥ
a samaḥ samavibhaktāṅgaḥ snigdhavarṇaḥ pratāpavān
c pīnavakṣā viśālākṣo lakṣmīvāñ śubhalakṣaṇaḥ
a dharmajñaḥ satyasaṃdhaś ca prajānāṃ ca hite rataḥ
c yaśasvī jñānasaṃpannaḥ śucir vaśyaḥ samādhimān
a rakṣitā jīvalokasya dharmasya parirakṣitā
c vedavedāṅgatattvajño dhanurvede ca niṣṭhitaḥ
a sarvaśāstrārthatattvajño smṛtimān pratibhānavān
c sarvalokapriyaḥ sādhur adīnātmā vicakṣaṇaḥ
a sarvadābhigataḥ sadbhiḥ samudra iva sindhubhiḥ
c āryaḥ sarvasamaś caiva sadaikapriyadarśanaḥ
a sa ca sarvaguṇopetaḥ kausalyānandavardhanaḥ
c samudra iva gāmbhīrye dhairyeṇa himavān iva
a viṣṇunā sadṛśo vīrye somavat priyadarśanaḥ
c kālāgnisadṛśaḥ krodhe kṣamayā pṛthivīsamaḥ
a dhanadena samas tyāge satye dharma ivāparaḥ
c tam evaṃguṇasaṃpannaṃ rāmaṃ satyaparākramam
a jyeṣṭhaṃ śreṣṭhaguṇair yuktaṃ priyaṃ daśarathaḥ sutam
c yauvarājyena saṃyoktum aicchat prītyā mahīpatiḥ
a tasyābhiṣekasaṃbhārān dṛṣṭvā bhāryātha kaikayī
c pūrvaṃ dattavarā devī varam enam ayācata
e vivāsanaṃ ca rāmasya bharatasyābhiṣecanam
a sa satyavacanād rājā dharmapāśena saṃyataḥ
c vivāsayām āsa sutaṃ rāmaṃ daśarathaḥ priyam
a sa jagāma vanaṃ vīraḥ pratijñām anupālayan
c pitur vacananirdeśāt kaikeyyāḥ priyakāraṇāt
a taṃ vrajantaṃ priyo bhrātā lakṣmaṇo 'nujagāma ha
c snehād vinayasaṃpannaḥ sumitrānandavardhanaḥ
a sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpannā nārīṇām uttamā vadhūḥ
c sītāpy anugatā rāmaṃ śaśinaṃ rohiṇī yathā
a paurair anugato dūraṃ pitrā daśarathena ca
c śṛṅgaverapure sūtaṃ gaṅgākūle vyasarjayat
a te vanena vanaṃ gatvā nadīs tīrtvā bahūdakāḥ
c citrakūṭam anuprāpya bharadvājasya śāsanāt
a ramyam āvasathaṃ kṛtvā ramamāṇā vane trayaḥ
c devagandharvasaṃkāśās tatra te nyavasan sukham
a citrakūṭaṃ gate rāme putraśokāturas tadā
c rājā daśarathaḥ svargaṃ jagāma vilapan sutam
a mṛte tu tasmin bharato vasiṣṭhapramukhair dvijaiḥ
c niyujyamāno rājyāya naicchad rājyaṃ mahābalaḥ
e sa jagāma vanaṃ vīro rāmapādaprasādakaḥ
a pāduke cāsya rājyāya nyāsaṃ dattvā punaḥ punaḥ
c nivartayām āsa tato bharataṃ bharatāgrajaḥ
a sa kāmam anavāpyaiva rāmapādāv upaspṛśan
c nandigrāme 'karod rājyaṃ rāmāgamanakāṅkṣayā
a rāmas tu punar ālakṣya nāgarasya janasya ca
c tatrāgamanam ekāgre daṇḍakān praviveśa ha
a virādhaṃ rākṣasaṃ hatvā śarabhaṅgaṃ dadarśa ha
c sutīkṣṇaṃ cāpy agastyaṃ ca agastya bhrātaraṃ tathā
a agastyavacanāc caiva jagrāhaindraṃ śarāsanam
c khaḍgaṃ ca paramaprītas tūṇī cākṣayasāyakau
a vasatas tasya rāmasya vane vanacaraiḥ saha
c ṛṣayo 'bhyāgaman sarve vadhāyāsurarakṣasām
a tena tatraiva vasatā janasthānanivāsinī
c virūpitā śūrpaṇakhā rākṣasī kāmarūpiṇī
a tataḥ śūrpaṇakhāvākyād udyuktān sarvarākṣasān
c kharaṃ triśirasaṃ caiva dūṣaṇaṃ caiva rākṣasaṃ
a nijaghāna raṇe rāmas teṣāṃ caiva padānugān
c rakṣasāṃ nihatāny āsan sahasrāṇi caturdaśa
a tato jñātivadhaṃ śrutvā rāvaṇaḥ krodhamūrchitaḥ
c sahāyaṃ varayām āsa mārīcaṃ nāma rākṣasaṃ
a vāryamāṇaḥ subahuśo mārīcena sa rāvaṇaḥ
c na virodho balavatā kṣamo rāvaṇa tena te
a anādṛtya tu tad vākyaṃ rāvaṇaḥ kālacoditaḥ
c jagāma sahamarīcas tasyāśramapadaṃ tadā
a tena māyāvinā dūram apavāhya nṛpātmajau
c jahāra bhāryāṃ rāmasya gṛdhraṃ hatvā jaṭāyuṣam
a gṛdhraṃ ca nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā hṛtāṃ śrutvā ca maithilīm
c rāghavaḥ śokasaṃtapto vilalāpākulendriyaḥ
a tatas tenaiva śokena gṛdhraṃ dagdhvā jaṭāyuṣam
c mārgamāṇo vane sītāṃ rākṣasaṃ saṃdadarśa ha
a kabandhaṃ nāma rūpeṇa vikṛtaṃ ghoradarśanam
c taṃ nihatya mahābāhur dadāha svargataś ca saḥ
a sa cāsya kathayām āsa śabarīṃ dharmacāriṇīm
c śramaṇīṃ dharmanipuṇām abhigaccheti rāghava
e so 'bhyagacchan mahātejāḥ śabarīṃ śatrusūdanaḥ
a śabaryā pūjitaḥ samyag rāmo daśarathātmajaḥ
c pampātīre hanumatā saṃgato vānareṇa ha
a hanumadvacanāc caiva sugrīveṇa samāgataḥ
c sugrīvāya ca tat sarvaṃ śaṃsad rāmo mahābalaḥ
a tato vānararājena vairānukathanaṃ prati
c rāmāyāveditaṃ sarvaṃ praṇayād duḥkhitena ca
e vālinaś ca balaṃ tatra kathayām āsa vānaraḥ
a pratijñātaṃ ca rāmeṇa tadā vālivadhaṃ prati
c sugrīvaḥ śaṅkitaś cāsīn nityaṃ vīryeṇa rāghave
a rāghavaḥ pratyayārthaṃ tu dundubheḥ kāyam uttamam
c pādāṅguṣṭhena cikṣepa saṃpūrṇaṃ daśayojanam
a bibheda ca punaḥ sālān saptaikena maheṣuṇā
c giriṃ rasātalaṃ caiva janayan pratyayaṃ tadā
a tataḥ prītamanās tena viśvastaḥ sa mahākapiḥ
c kiṣkindhāṃ rāmasahito jagāma ca guhāṃ tadā
a tato 'garjad dharivaraḥ sugrīvo hemapiṅgalaḥ
c tena nādena mahatā nirjagāma harīśvaraḥ
a tataḥ sugrīvavacanād dhatvā vālinam āhave
c sugrīvam eva tad rājye rāghavaḥ pratyapādayat
a sa ca sarvān samānīya vānarān vānararṣabhaḥ
c diśaḥ prasthāpayām āsa didṛkṣur janakātmajām
a tato gṛdhrasya vacanāt saṃpāter hanumān balī
c śatayojanavistīrṇaṃ pupluve lavaṇārṇavam
a tatra laṅkāṃ samāsādya purīṃ rāvaṇapālitām
c dadarśa sītāṃ dhyāyantīm aśokavanikāṃ gatām
a nivedayitvābhijñānaṃ pravṛttiṃ ca nivedya ca
c samāśvāsya ca vaidehīṃ mardayām āsa toraṇam
a pañca senāgragān hatvā sapta mantrisutān api
c śūram akṣaṃ ca niṣpiṣya grahaṇaṃ samupāgamat
a astreṇonmuham ātmānaṃ jñātvā paitāmahād varāt
c marṣayan rākṣasān vīro yantriṇas tān yadṛcchayā
a tato dagdhvā purīṃ laṅkām ṛte sītāṃ ca maithilīm
c rāmāya priyam ākhyātuṃ punar āyān mahākapiḥ
a so 'bhigamya mahātmānaṃ kṛtvā rāmaṃ pradakṣiṇam
c nyavedayad ameyātmā dṛṣṭā sīteti tattvataḥ
a tataḥ sugrīvasahito gatvā tīraṃ mahodadheḥ
c samudraṃ kṣobhayām āsa śarair ādityasaṃnibhaiḥ
a darśayām āsa cātmānaṃ samudraḥ saritāṃ patiḥ
c samudravacanāc caiva nalaṃ setum akārayat
a tena gatvā purīṃ laṅkāṃ hatvā rāvaṇam āhave
c abhyaṣiñcat sa laṅkāyāṃ rākṣasendraṃ vibhīṣaṇam
a karmaṇā tena mahatā trailokyaṃ sacarācaram
c sadevarṣigaṇaṃ tuṣṭaṃ rāghavasya mahātmanaḥ
a tathā paramasaṃtuṣṭaiḥ pūjitaḥ sarvadaivataiḥ
c kṛtakṛtyas tadā rāmo vijvaraḥ pramumoda ha
a devatābhyo varān prāpya samutthāpya ca vānarān
c puṣpakaṃ tat samāruhya nandigrāmaṃ yayau tadā
a nandigrāme jaṭāṃ hitvā bhrātṛbhiḥ sahito 'naghaḥ
c rāmaḥ sītām anuprāpya rājyaṃ punar avāptavān
a prahṛṣṭamudito lokas tuṣṭaḥ puṣṭaḥ sudhārmikaḥ
c nirāyamo arogaś ca durbhikṣabhayavarjitaḥ
a na putramaraṇaṃ ke cid drakṣyanti puruṣāḥ kva cit
c nāryaś cāvidhavā nityaṃ bhaviṣyanti pativratāḥ
a na vātajaṃ bhayaṃ kiṃ cin nāpsu majjanti jantavaḥ
c na cāgrijaṃ bhayaṃ kiṃ cid yathā kṛtayuge tathā
a aśvamedhaśatair iṣṭvā tathā bahusuvarṇakaiḥ
c gavāṃ koṭyayutaṃ dattvā vidvadbhyo vidhipūrvakam
a rājavaṃśāñ śataguṇān sthāpayiṣyati rāghavaḥ
c cāturvarṇyaṃ ca loke 'smin sve sve dharme niyokṣyati
a daśavarṣasahasrāṇi daśavarṣaśatāni ca
c rāmo rājyam upāsitvā brahmalokaṃ gamiṣyati
a idaṃ pavitraṃ pāpaghnaṃ puṇyaṃ vedaiś ca saṃmitam
c yaḥ paṭhed rāmacaritaṃ sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate
a etad ākhyānam āyuṣyaṃ paṭhan rāmāyaṇaṃ naraḥ
c saputrapautraḥ sagaṇaḥ pretya svarge mahīyate
a paṭhan dvijo vāgṛṣabhatvam īyāt
syāt kṣatriyo bhūmipatitvam īyāt
c vaṇigjanaḥ paṇyaphalatvam īyāj
janaś ca śūdro 'pi mahattvam īyāt
a nāradasya tu tad vākyaṃ śrutvā vākyaviśāradaḥ
c pūjayām āsa dharmātmā sahaśiṣyo mahāmuniḥ
a yathāvat pūjitas tena devarṣir nāradas tadā
c āpṛṣṭvaivābhyanujñātaḥ sa jagāma vihāyasaṃ
a sa muhūtaṃ gate tasmin devalokaṃ munis tadā
c jagāma tamasātīraṃ jāhnavyās tv avidūrataḥ
a sa tu tīraṃ samāsādya tamasāyā mahāmuniḥ
c śiṣyam āha sthitaṃ pārśve dṛṣṭvā tīrtham akardamam
a akardamam idaṃ tīrthaṃ bharadvāja niśāmaya
c ramaṇīyaṃ prasannāmbu sanmanuṣyamano yathā
a nyasyatāṃ kalaśas tāta dīyatāṃ valkalaṃ mama
c idam evāvagāhiṣye tamasātīrtham uttamam
a evam ukto bharadvājo vālmīkena mahātmanā
c prāyacchata munes tasya valkalaṃ niyato guroḥ
a sa śiṣyahastād ādāya valkalaṃ niyatendriyaḥ
c vicacāra ha paśyaṃs tat sarvato vipulaṃ vanam
a tasyābhyāśe tu mithunaṃ carantam anapāyinam
c dadarśa bhagavāṃs tatra krauñcayoś cāruniḥsvanam
a tasmāt tu mithunād ekaṃ pumāṃsaṃ pāpaniścayaḥ
c jaghāna vairanilayo niṣādas tasya paśyataḥ
a taṃ śoṇitaparītāṅgaṃ veṣṭamānaṃ mahītale
c bhāryā tu nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā rurāva karuṇāṃ giram
a tathā tu taṃ dvijaṃ dṛṣṭvā niṣādena nipātitam
c ṛṣer dharmātmanas tasya kāruṇyaṃ samapadyata
a tataḥ karuṇaveditvād adharmo 'yam iti dvijaḥ
c niśāmya rudatīṃ krauñcīm idaṃ vacanam abravīt
a mā niṣāda pratiṣṭhāṃ tvam agamaḥ śāśvatīṃ samāḥ
c yat krauñcamithunād ekam avadhīḥ kāmamohitam
a tasyaivaṃ bruvataś cintā babhūva hṛdi vīkṣataḥ
c śokārtenāsya śakuneḥ kim idaṃ vyāhṛtaṃ mayā
a cintayan sa mahāprājñaś cakāra matimān matim
c śiṣyaṃ caivābravīd vākyam idaṃ sa munipuṃgavaḥ
a pādabaddho 'kṣarasamas tantrīlayasamanvitaḥ
c śokārtasya pravṛtto me śloko bhavatu nānyathā
a śiṣyas tu tasya bruvato muner vākyam anuttamam
c pratijagrāha saṃhṛṣṭas tasya tuṣṭo 'bhavad guruḥ
a so 'bhiṣekaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā tīrthe tasmin yathāvidhi
c tam eva cintayann artham upāvartata vai muniḥ
a bharadvājas tataḥ śiṣyo vinītaḥ śrutavān guroḥ
c kalaśaṃ pūrṇam ādāya pṛṣṭhato 'nujagāma ha
a sa praviśyāśramapadaṃ śiṣyeṇa saha dharmavit
c upaviṣṭaḥ kathāś cānyāś cakāra dhyānam āsthitaḥ
a ājagāma tato brahmā lokakartā svayaṃprabhuḥ
c caturmukho mahātejā draṣṭuṃ taṃ munipuṃgavam
a vālmīkir atha taṃ dṛṣṭvā sahasotthāya vāg yataḥ
c prāñjaliḥ prayato bhūtvā tasthau paramavismitaḥ
a pūjayām āsa taṃ devaṃ pādyārghyāsanavandanaiḥ
c praṇamya vidhivac cainaṃ pṛṣṭvānāmayam avyayam
a athopaviśya bhagavān āsane paramārcite
c vālmīkaye maharṣaye saṃdideśāsanaṃ tataḥ
a upaviṣṭe tadā tasmin sākṣāl lokapitāmahe
c tad gatenaiva manasā vālmīkir dhyānam āsthitaḥ
a pāpātmanā kṛtaṃ kaṣṭaṃ vairagrahaṇabuddhinā
c yas tādṛśaṃ cāruravaṃ krauñcaṃ hanyād akāraṇāt
a śocann eva muhuḥ krauñcīm upaślokam imaṃ punaḥ
c jagāv antargatamanā bhūtvā śokaparāyaṇaḥ
a tam uvāca tato brahmā prahasan munipuṃgavam
c śloka eva tvayā baddho nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
a macchandād eva te brahman pravṛtteyaṃ sarasvatī
c rāmasya caritaṃ kṛtsnaṃ kuru tvam ṛṣisattama
a dharmātmano guṇavato loke rāmasya dhīmataḥ
c vṛttaṃ kathaya dhīrasya yathā te nāradāc chrutam
a rahasyaṃ ca prakāśaṃ ca yad vṛttaṃ tasya dhīmataḥ
c rāmasya saha saumitre rākṣasānāṃ ca sarvaśaḥ
a vaidehyāś caiva yad vṛttaṃ prakāśaṃ yadi vā rahaḥ
c tac cāpy aviditaṃ sarvaṃ viditaṃ te bhaviṣyati
a na te vāg anṛtā kāvye kā cid atra bhaviṣyati
c kuru rāma kathāṃ puṇyāṃ ślokabaddhāṃ manoramām
a yāvat sthāsyanti girayaḥ saritaś ca mahītale
c tāvad rāmāyaṇakathā lokeṣu pracariṣyati
a yāvad rāmasya ca kathā tvatkṛtā pracariṣyati
c tāvad ūrdhvam adhaś ca tvaṃ mallokeṣu nivatsyasi
a ity uktvā bhagavān brahmā tatraivāntaradhīyata
c tataḥ saśiṣyo vālmīkir munir vismayam āyayau
a tasya śiṣyās tataḥ sarve jaguḥ ślokam imaṃ punaḥ
c muhur muhuḥ prīyamāṇāḥ prāhuś ca bhṛśavismitāḥ
a samākṣaraiś caturbhir yaḥ pādair gīto maharṣiṇā
c so 'nuvyāharaṇād bhūyaḥ śokaḥ ślokatvam āgataḥ
a tasya buddhir iyaṃ jātā vālmīker bhāvitātmanaḥ
c kṛtsnaṃ rāmāyaṇaṃ kāvyam īdṛśaiḥ karavāṇy aham
a udāravṛttārthapadair manoramais
tadāsya rāmasya cakāra kīrtimān
c samākṣaraiḥ ślokaśatair yaśasvino
yaśaskaraṃ kāvyam udāradhīr muniḥ
a śrutvā vas tu samagraṃ tad dharmātmā dharmasaṃhitam
c vyaktam anveṣate bhūyo yad vṛttaṃ tasya dhīmataḥ
a upaspṛśyodakaṃ saṃyan muniḥ sthitvā kṛtāñjaliḥ
c prācīnāgreṣu darbheṣu dharmeṇānveṣate gatim
a janma rāmasya sumahad vīryaṃ sarvānukūlatām
c lokasya priyatāṃ kṣāntiṃ saumyatāṃ satyaśīlatām
a nānācitrāḥ kathāś cānyā viśvāmitrasahāyane
c jānakyāś ca vivāhaṃ ca dhanuṣaś ca vibhedanam
a rāmarāmavivādaṃ ca guṇān dāśarathes tathā
c tathābhiṣekaṃ rāmasya kaikeyyā duṣṭabhāvatām
a vyāghātaṃ cābhiṣekasya rāmasya ca vivāsanam
c rājñaḥ śokaṃ vilāpaṃ ca paralokasya cāśrayam
a prakṛtīnāṃ viṣādaṃ ca prakṛtīnāṃ visarjanam
c niṣādādhipasaṃvādaṃ sūtopāvartanaṃ tathā
a gaṅgāyāś cābhisaṃtāraṃ bharadvājasya darśanam
c bharadvājābhyanujñānāc citrakūṭasya darśanam
a vāstukarmaniveśaṃ ca bharatāgamanaṃ tathā
c prasādanaṃ ca rāmasya pituś ca salilakriyām
a pādukāgryābhiṣekaṃ ca nandigrāma nivāsanam
c daṇḍakāraṇyagamanaṃ sutīkṣṇena samāgamam
a anasūyāsamasyāṃ ca aṅgarāgasya cārpaṇam
c śūrpaṇakhyāś ca saṃvādaṃ virūpakaraṇaṃ tathā
a vadhaṃ kharatriśirasor utthānaṃ rāvaṇasya ca
c mārīcasya vadhaṃ caiva vaidehyā haraṇaṃ tathā
a rāghavasya vilāpaṃ ca gṛdhrarājanibarhaṇam
c kabandhadarśanaṃ caiva pampāyāś cāpi darśanam
a śarbaryā darśanaṃ caiva hanūmaddarśanaṃ tathā
c vilāpaṃ caiva pampāyāṃ rāghavasya mahātmanaḥ
a ṛṣyamūkasya gamanaṃ sugrīveṇa samāgamam
c pratyayotpādanaṃ sakhyaṃ vālisugrīvavigraham
a vālipramathanaṃ caiva sugrīvapratipādanam
c tārāvilāpasamayaṃ varṣarātrinivāsanam
a kopaṃ rāghavasiṃhasya balānām upasaṃgraham
c diśaḥ prasthāpanaṃ caiva pṛthivyāś ca nivedanam
a aṅgulīyakadānaṃ ca ṛkṣasya biladarśanam
c prāyopaveśanaṃ caiva saṃpāteś cāpi darśanam
a parvatārohaṇaṃ caiva sāgarasya ca laṅghanam
c rātrau laṅkāpraveśaṃ ca ekasyāpi vicintanam
a āpānabhūmigamanam avarodhasya darśanam
c aśokavanikāyānaṃ sītāyāś cāpi darśanam
a abhijñānapradānaṃ ca sītāyāś cāpi bhāṣaṇam
c rākṣasītarjanaṃ caiva trijaṭāsvapnadarśanam
a maṇipradānaṃ sītāyā vṛkṣabhaṅgaṃ tathaiva ca
c rākṣasīvidravaṃ caiva kiṃkarāṇāṃ nibarhaṇam
a grahaṇaṃ vāyusūnoś ca laṅkādāhābhigarjanam
c pratiplavanam evātha madhūnāṃ haraṇaṃ tathā
a rāghavāśvāsanaṃ caiva maṇiniryātanaṃ tathā
c saṃgamaṃ ca samudrasya nalasetoś ca bandhanam
a pratāraṃ ca samudrasya rātrau laṅkāvarodhanam
c vibhīṣaṇena saṃsargaṃ vadhopāyanivedanam
a kumbhakarṇasya nidhanaṃ meghanādanibarhaṇam
c rāvaṇasya vināśaṃ ca sītāvāptim areḥ pure
a bibhīṣaṇābhiṣekaṃ ca puṣpakasya ca darśanam
c ayodhyāyāś ca gamanaṃ bharatena samāgamam
a rāmābhiṣekābhyudayaṃ sarvasainyavisarjanam
c svarāṣṭrarañjanaṃ caiva vaidehyāś ca visarjanam
a anāgataṃ ca yat kiṃ cid rāmasya vasudhātale
c tac cakārottare kāvye vālmīkir bhagavān ṛṣiḥ
a prāptarājyasya rāmasya vālmīkir bhagavān ṛṣiḥ
c cakāra caritaṃ kṛtsnaṃ vicitrapadam ātmavān
a kṛtvā tu tan mahāprājñaḥ sabhaviṣyaṃ sahottaram
c cintayām āsa ko nv etat prayuñjīyād iti prabhuḥ
a tasya cintayamānasya maharṣer bhāvitātmanaḥ
c agṛhṇītāṃ tataḥ pādau muniveṣau kuśīlavau
a kuśīlavau tu dharmajñau rājaputrau yaśasvinau
c bhrātarau svarasaṃpannau dadarśāśramavāsinau
a sa tu medhāvinau dṛṣṭvā vedeṣu pariniṣṭhitau
c vedopabṛhmaṇārthāya tāv agrāhayata prabhuḥ
a kāvyaṃ rāmāyaṇaṃ kṛtsnaṃ sītāyāś caritaṃ mahat
c paulastya vadham ity eva cakāra caritavrataḥ
a pāṭhye geye ca madhuraṃ pramāṇais tribhir anvitam
c jātibhiḥ saptabhir yuktaṃ tantrīlayasamanvitam
a hāsyaśṛṅgārakāruṇyaraudravīrabhayānakaiḥ
c bībhatsādirasair yuktaṃ kāvyam etad agāyatām
a tau tu gāndharvatattvajñau sthāna mūrcchana kovidau
c bhrātarau svarasaṃpannau gandharvāv iva rūpiṇau
a rūpalakṣaṇasaṃpannau madhurasvarabhāṣiṇau
c bimbād ivoddhṛtau bimbau rāmadehāt tathāparau
a tau rājaputrau kārtsnyena dharmyam ākhyānam uttamam
c vāco vidheyaṃ tat sarvaṃ kṛtvā kāvyam aninditau
a ṛṣīṇāṃ ca dvijātīnāṃ sādhūnāṃ ca samāgame
c yathopadeśaṃ tattvajñau jagatus tau samāhitau
e mahātmānau mahābhāgau sarvalakṣaṇalakṣitau
a tau kadā cit sametānām ṛṣīṇāṃ bhāvitātmanām
c āsīnānāṃ samīpasthāv idaṃ kāvyam agāyatām
a tac chrutvā munayaḥ sarve bāṣpaparyākulekṣaṇāḥ
c sādhu sādhv ity tāv ūcatuḥ paraṃ vismayam āgatāḥ
a te prītamanasaḥ sarve munayo dharmavatsalāḥ
c praśaśaṃsuḥ praśastavyau gāyamānau kuśīlavau
a aho gītasya mādhuryaṃ ślokānāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ
c ciranirvṛttam apy etat pratyakṣam iva darśitam
a praviśya tāv ubhau suṣṭhu tadā bhāvam agāyatām
c sahitau madhuraṃ raktaṃ saṃpannaṃ svarasaṃpadā
a evaṃ praśasyamānau tau tapaḥślāghyair maharṣibhiḥ
c saṃraktataram atyarthaṃ madhuraṃ tāv agāyatām
a prītaḥ kaś cin munis tābhyāṃ saṃsthitaḥ kalaśaṃ dadau
c prasanno valkalaṃ kaś cid dadau tābhyāṃ mahāyaśāḥ
a āścaryam idam ākhyānaṃ muninā saṃprakīrtitam
c paraṃ kavīnām ādhāraṃ samāptaṃ ca yathākramam
a praśasyamānau sarvatra kadā cit tatra gāyakau
c rathyāsu rājamārgeṣu dadarśa bharatāgrajaḥ
a svaveśma cānīya tato bhrātarau sakuśīlavau
c pūjayām āsa pūjārhau rāmaḥ śatrunibarhaṇaḥ
a āsīnaḥ kāñcane divye sa ca siṃhāsane prabhuḥ
c upopaviṣṭaiḥ sacivair bhrātṛbhiś ca paraṃtapaḥ
a dṛṣṭvā tu rūpasaṃpannau tāv ubhau vīṇinau tataḥ
c uvāca lakṣmaṇaṃ rāmaḥ śatrughnaṃ bharataṃ tathā
a śrūyatām idam ākhyānam anayor devavarcasoḥ
c vicitrārthapadaṃ samyag gāyator madhurasvaram
a imau munī pārthivalakṣmaṇānvitau
kuśīlavau caiva mahātapasvinau
c mamāpi tad bhūtikaraṃ pracakṣate
mahānubhāvaṃ caritaṃ nibodhata
a tatas tu tau rāmavacaḥ pracoditāv
agāyatāṃ mārgavidhānasaṃpadā
c sa cāpi rāmaḥ pariṣadgataḥ śanair
bubhūṣayāsaktamanā babhūva
a sarvāpūrvam iyaṃ yeṣām āsīt kṛtsnā vasuṃdharā
c prajāpatim upādāya nṛpāṇāṃ jayaśālinām
a yeṣāṃ sa sagaro nāma sāgaro yena khānitaḥ
c ṣaṣṭiḥ putrasahasrāṇi yaṃ yāntaṃ paryavārayan
a ikṣvākūṇām idaṃ teṣāṃ rājñāṃ vaṃśe mahātmanām
c mahad utpannam ākhyānaṃ rāmāyaṇam iti śrutam
a tad idaṃ vartayiṣyāmi sarvaṃ nikhilam āditaḥ
c dharmakāmārthasahitaṃ śrotavyam anasūyayā
a kosalo nāma muditaḥ sphīto janapado mahān
c niviṣṭaḥ sarayūtīre prabhūtadhanadhānyavān
a ayodhyā nāma nagarī tatrāsīl lokaviśrutā
c manunā mānavendreṇa yā purī nirmitā svayam
a āyatā daśa ca dve ca yojanāni mahāpurī
c śrīmatī trīṇi vistīrṇā suvibhaktamahāpathā
a rājamārgeṇa mahatā suvibhaktena śobhitā
c muktapuṣpāvakīrṇena jalasiktena nityaśaḥ
a tāṃ tu rājā daśaratho mahārāṣṭravivardhanaḥ
c purīm āvāsayām āsa divi devapatir yathā
a kapāṭatoraṇavatīṃ suvibhaktāntarāpaṇām
c sarvayantrāyudhavatīm upetāṃ sarvaśilpibhiḥ
a sūtamāgadhasaṃbādhāṃ śrīmatīm atulaprabhām
c uccāṭṭāladhvajavatīṃ śataghnīśatasaṃkulām
a vadhūnāṭakasaṅghaiś ca saṃyuktāṃ sarvataḥ purīm
c udyānāmravaṇopetāṃ mahatīṃ sālamekhalām
a durgagambhīraparighāṃ durgām anyair durāsadām
c vājivāraṇasaṃpūrṇāṃ gobhir uṣṭraiḥ kharais tathā
a sāmantarājasaṅghaiś ca balikarmabhir āvṛtām
c nānādeśanivāsaiś ca vaṇigbhir upaśobhitām
a prasādai ratnavikṛtaiḥ parvatair upaśobhitām
c kūṭāgāraiś ca saṃpūrṇām indrasyevāmarāvatīm
a citrām aṣṭāpadākārāṃ varanārīgaṇair yutām
c sarvaratnasamākīrṇāṃ vimānagṛhaśobhitām
a gṛhagāḍhām avicchidrāṃ samabhūmau niveśitām
c śālitaṇḍulasaṃpūrṇām ikṣukāṇḍarasodakām
a dundubhībhir mṛdaṅgaiś ca vīṇābhiḥ paṇavais tathā
c nāditāṃ bhṛśam atyarthaṃ pṛthivyāṃ tām anuttamām
a vimānam iva siddhānāṃ tapasādhigataṃ divi
c suniveśitaveśmāntāṃ narottamasamāvṛtām
a ye ca bāṇair na vidhyanti viviktam aparāparam
c śabdavedhyaṃ ca vitataṃ laghuhastā viśāradāḥ
a siṃhavyāghravarāhāṇāṃ mattānāṃ nadatāṃ vane
c hantāro niśitaiḥ śastrair balād bāhubalair api
a tādṛśānāṃ sahasrais tām abhipūrṇāṃ mahārathaiḥ
c purīm āvāsayām āsa rājā daśarathas tadā
a tām agnimadbhir guṇavadbhir āvṛtāṃ
dvijottamair vedaṣaḍaṅgapāragaiḥ
c sahasradaiḥ satyaratair mahātmabhir
maharṣikalpair ṛṣibhiś ca kevalaiḥ
a puryāṃ tasyām ayodhyāyāṃ vedavit sarvasaṃgrahaḥ
c dīrghadarśī mahātejāḥ paurajānapadapriyaḥ
a ikṣvākūṇām atiratho yajvā dharmarato vaśī
c maharṣikalpo rājarṣis triṣu lokṛṣu viśrutaḥ
a balavān nihatāmitro mitravān vijitendriyaḥ
c dhanaiś ca saṃcayaiś cānyaiḥ śakravaiśravaṇopamaḥ
a yathā manur mahātejā lokasya parirakṣitā
c tathā daśaratho rājā vasañ jagad apālayat
a tena satyābhisaṃdhena trivargam anutiṣṭhatā
c pālitā sā purī śreṣṭhendreṇa ivāmarāvatī
a tasmin puravare hṛṣṭā dharmātmanā bahu śrutāḥ
c narās tuṣṭādhanaiḥ svaiḥ svair alubdhāḥ satyavādinaḥ
a nālpasaṃnicayaḥ kaś cid āsīt tasmin purottame
c kuṭumbī yo hy asiddhārtho 'gavāśvadhanadhānyavān
a kāmī vā na kadaryo vā nṛśaṃsaḥ puruṣaḥ kva cit
c draṣṭuṃ śakyam ayodhyāyāṃ nāvidvān na ca nāstikaḥ
a sarve narāś ca nāryaś ca dharmaśīlāḥ susaṃyatāḥ
c muditāḥ śīlavṛttābhyāṃ maharṣaya ivāmalāḥ
a nākuṇḍalī nāmukuṭī nāsragvī nālpabhogavān
c nāmṛṣṭo nānuliptāṅgo nāsugandhaś ca vidyate
a nāmṛṣṭabhojī nādātā nāpy anaṅgadaniṣkadhṛk
c nāhastābharaṇo vāpi dṛśyate nāpy anātmavān
a nānāhitāgnir nāyajvā vipro nāpy asahasradaḥ
c kaś cid āsīd ayodhyāyāṃ na ca nirvṛttasaṃkaraḥ
a svakarmaniratā nityaṃ brāhmaṇā vijitendriyāḥ
c dānādhyayanaśīlāś ca saṃyatāś ca pratigrahe
a na nāstiko nānṛtako na kaś cid abahuśrutaḥ
c nāsūyako na cāśakto nāvidvān vidyate tadā
a na dīnaḥ kṣiptacitto vā vyathito vāpi kaś cana
c kaś cin naro vā nārī vā nāśrīmān nāpy arūpavān
e draṣṭuṃ śakyam ayodhyāyāṃ nāpi rājanyabhaktimān
a varṇeṣv agryacaturtheṣu devatātithipūjakāḥ
c dīrghāyuṣo narāḥ sarve dharmaṃ satyaṃ ca saṃśritāḥ
a kṣatraṃ brahmamukhaṃ cāsīd vaiśyāḥ kṣatram anuvratāḥ
c śūdrāḥ svadharmaniratās trīn varṇān upacāriṇaḥ
a sā tenekṣvākunāthena purī suparirakṣitā
c yathā purastān manunā mānavendreṇa dhīmatā
a yodhānām agnikalpānāṃ peśalānām amarṣiṇām
c saṃpūrṇākṛtavidyānāṃ guhākesariṇām iva
a kāmbojaviṣaye jātair bāhlīkaiś ca hayottamaiḥ
c vanāyujair nadījaiś ca pūrṇāharihayopamaiḥ
a vindhyaparvapajair mattaiḥ pūrṇā haimavatair api
c madānvitair atibalair mātaṅgaiḥ parvatopamaiḥ
a añjanād api niṣkrāntair vāmanād api ca dvipaiḥ
c bhadramandrair bhadramṛgair mṛgamandraiś ca sā purī
a nityamattaiḥ sadā pūrṇā nāgair acalasaṃnibhaiḥ
c sā yojane ca dve bhūyaḥ satyanāmā prakāśate
a tāṃ satyanāmāṃ dṛḍhatoraṇārgalām
gṛhair vicitrair upaśobhitāṃ śivām
c purīm ayodhyāṃ nṛsahasrasaṃkulāṃ
śaśāsa vai śakrasamo mahīpatiḥ
a aṣṭau babhūvur vīrasya tasyāmātyā yaśasvinaḥ
c śucayaś cānuraktāś ca rājakṛtyeṣu nityaśaḥ
a dhṛṣṭir jayanto vijayaḥ siddhārtho arthasādhakaḥ
c aśoko mantrapālaś ca sumantraś cāṣṭamo 'bhavat
a ṛtvijau dvāv abhimatau tasyāstām ṛṣisattamau
c vasiṣṭho vāmadevaś ca mantriṇaś ca tathāpare
a śrīmantaś ca mahātmānaḥ śāstrajñā dṛḍhavikramāḥ
c kīrtimantaḥ praṇihitā yathā vacanakāriṇaḥ
a tejaḥkṣamāyaśaḥprāptāḥ smitapūrvābhibhāṣiṇaḥ
c krodhāt kāmārthahetor vā na brūyur anṛtaṃ vacaḥ
a teṣām aviditaṃ kiṃ cit sveṣu nāsti pareṣu vā
c kriyamāṇaṃ kṛtaṃ vāpi cāreṇāpi cikīrṣitam
a kuśalā vyavahāreṣu sauhṛdeṣu parīkṣitāḥ
c prāptakālaṃ yathā daṇḍaṃ dhārayeyuḥ suteṣv api
a kośasaṃgrahaṇe yuktā balasya ca parigrahe
c ahitaṃ cāpi puruṣaṃ na vihiṃsyur adūṣakam
a vīrāṃś ca niyatotsāhā rāja śāstram anuṣṭhitāḥ
c śucīnāṃ rakṣitāraś ca nityaṃ viṣayavāsinām
a brahmakṣatram ahiṃsantas te kośaṃ samapūrayan
c sutīkṣṇadaṇḍāḥ saṃprekṣya puruṣasya balābalam
a śucīnām ekabuddhīnāṃ sarveṣāṃ saṃprajānatām
c nāsīt pure vā rāṣṭre vā mṛṣāvādī naraḥ kva cit
a kaś cin na duṣṭas tatrāsīt paradāraratir naraḥ
c praśāntaṃ sarvam evāsīd rāṣṭraṃ puravaraṃ ca tat
a suvāsasaḥ suveśāś ca te ca sarve suśīlinaḥ
c hitārthaṃ ca narendrasya jāgrato nayacakṣuṣā
a gurau guṇagṛhītāś ca prakhyātāś ca parākramaiḥ
c videśeṣv api vijñātāḥ sarvato buddhiniścayāt
a īdṛśais tair amātyais tu rājā daśaratho 'naghaḥ
c upapanno guṇopetair anvaśāsad vasuṃdharām
a avekṣamāṇaś cāreṇa prajā dharmeṇa rañjayan
c nādhyagacchad viśiṣṭaṃ vā tulyaṃ vā śatrum ātmanaḥ
a tair mantribhir mantrahitair niviṣṭair
vṛto 'nuraktaiḥ kuśalaiḥ samarthaiḥ
c sa pārthivo dīptim avāpa yuktas
tejomayair gobhir ivodito 'rkaḥ
a tasya tv evaṃ prabhāvasya dharmajñasya mahātmanaḥ
c sutārthaṃ tapyamānasya nāsīd vaṃśakaraḥ sutaḥ
a cintayānasya tasyaivaṃ buddhir āsīn mahātmanaḥ
c sutārthaṃ vājimedhena kimarthaṃ na yajāmy aham
a sa niścitāṃ matiṃ kṛtvā yaṣṭavyam iti buddhimān
c mantribhiḥ saha dharmātmā sarvair eva kṛtātmabhiḥ
a tato 'bravīd idaṃ rājā sumantraṃ mantrisattamam
c śīghram ānaya me sarvān gurūṃs tān sapurohitān
a etac chrutvā rahaḥ sūto rājānam idam abravīt
c ṛtvigbhir upadiṣṭo 'yaṃ purāvṛtto mayā śrutaḥ
a sanatkumāro bhagavān pūrvaṃ kathitavān kathām
c ṛṣīṇāṃ saṃnidhau rājaṃs tava putrāgamaṃ prati
a kāśyapasya tu putro 'sti vibhāṇḍaka iti śrutaḥ
c ṛṣyaśṛṅga iti khyātas tasya putro bhaviṣyati
a sa vane nityasaṃvṛddho munir vanacaraḥ sadā
c nānyaṃ jānāti viprendro nityaṃ pitranuvartanāt
a dvaividhyaṃ brahmacaryasya bhaviṣyati mahātmanaḥ
c lokeṣu prathitaṃ rājan vipraiś ca kathitaṃ sadā
a tasyaivaṃ vartamānasya kālaḥ samabhivartata
c agniṃ śuśrūṣamāṇasya pitaraṃ ca yaśasvinam
a etasminn eva kāle tu romapādaḥ pratāpavān
c aṅgeṣu prathitā rājā bhaviṣyati mahābalaḥ
a tasya vyatikramād rājño bhaviṣyati sudāruṇā
c anāvṛṣṭiḥ sughorā vai sarvabhūtabhayāvahā
a anāvṛṣṭyāṃ tu vṛttāyāṃ rājā duḥkhasamanvitaḥ
c brāhmaṇāñ śrutavṛddhāṃś ca samānīya pravakṣyati
a bhavantaḥ śrutadharmāṇo loke cāritravedinaḥ
c samādiśantu niyamaṃ prāyaścittaṃ yathā bhavet
a vakṣyanti te mahīpālaṃ brāhmaṇā vedapāragāḥ
c vibhāṇḍakasutaṃ rājan sarvopāyair ihānaya
a ānāyya ca mahīpāla ṛṣyaśṛṅgaṃ susatkṛtam
c prayaccha kanyāṃ śāntāṃ vai vidhinā susamāhitaḥ
a teṣāṃ tu vacanaṃ śrutvā rājā cintāṃ prapatsyate
c kenopāyena vai śakyam ihānetuṃ sa vīryavān
a tato rājā viniścitya saha mantribhir ātmavān
c purohitam amātyāṃś ca preṣayiṣyati satkṛtān
a te tu rājño vacaḥ śrutvā vyathitā vanatānanāḥ
c na gacchema ṛṣer bhītā anuneṣyanti taṃ nṛpam
a vakṣyanti cintayitvā te tasyopāyāṃś ca tān kṣamān
c āneṣyāmo vayaṃ vipraṃ na ca doṣo bhaviṣyati
a evam aṅgādhipenaiva gaṇikābhir ṛṣeḥ sutaḥ
c ānīto 'varṣayad devaḥ śāntā cāsmai pradīyate
a ṛṣyaśṛṅgas tu jāmātā putrāṃs tava vidhāsyati
c sanatkumārakathitam etāvad vyāhṛtaṃ mayā
a atha hṛṣṭo daśarathaḥ sumantraṃ pratyabhāṣata
c yatharṣyaśṛṅgas tv ānīto vistareṇa tvayocyatām
a sumantraś codito rājñā provācedaṃ vacas tadā
c yatharṣyaśṛṅgas tv ānītaḥ śṛṇu me mantribhiḥ saha
a romapādam uvācedaṃ sahāmātyaḥ purohitaḥ
c upāyo nirapāyo 'yam asmābhir abhicintitaḥ
a ṛṣyaśṛṅgo vanacaras tapaḥsvādhyāyane rataḥ
c anabhijñaḥ sa nārīṇāṃ viṣayāṇāṃ sukhasya ca
a indriyārthair abhimatair naracitta pramāthibhiḥ
c puram ānāyayiṣyāmaḥ kṣipraṃ cādhyavasīyatām
a gaṇikās tatra gacchantu rūpavatyaḥ svalaṃkṛtāḥ
c pralobhya vividhopāyair āneṣyantīha satkṛtāḥ
a śrutvā tatheti rājā ca pratyuvāca purohitam
c purohito mantriṇaś ca tathā cakruś ca te tadā
a vāramukhyās tu tac chrutvā vanaṃ praviviśur mahat
c āśramasyāvidūre 'smin yatnaṃ kurvanti darśane
a ṛṣiputrasya ghorasya nityam āśramavāsinaḥ
c pituḥ sa nityasaṃtuṣṭo nāticakrāma cāśramāt
a na tena janmaprabhṛti dṛṣṭapūrvaṃ tapasvinā
c strī vā pumān vā yac cānyat sattvaṃ nagara rāṣṭrajam
a tataḥ kadā cit taṃ deśam ājagāma yadṛcchayā
c vibhāṇḍakasutas tatra tāś cāpaśyad varāṅganāḥ
a tāś citraveṣāḥ pramadā gāyantyo madhurasvaraiḥ
c ṛṣiputram upāgamya sarvā vacanam abruvan
a kas tvaṃ kiṃ vartase brahmañ jñātum icchāmahe vayam
c ekas tvaṃ vijane ghore vane carasi śaṃsa naḥ
a adṛṣṭarūpās tās tena kāmyarūpā vane striyaḥ
c hārdāt tasya matir jātā ākhyātuṃ pitaraṃ svakam
a pitā vibhāṇḍako 'smākaṃ tasyāhaṃ suta aurasaḥ
c ṛṣyaśṛṅga iti khyātaṃ nāma karma ca me bhuvi
a ihāśramapado 'smākaṃ samīpe śubhadarśanāḥ
c kariṣye vo 'tra pūjāṃ vai sarveṣāṃ vidhipūrvakam
a ṛṣiputravacaḥ śrutvā sarvāsāṃ matir āsa vai
c tad āśramapadaṃ draṣṭuṃ jagmuḥ sarvāś ca tena ha
a gatānāṃ tu tataḥ pūjām ṛṣiputraś cakāra ha
c idam arghyam idaṃ pādyam idaṃ mūlaṃ phalaṃ ca naḥ
a pratigṛhya tu tāṃ pūjāṃ sarvā eva samutsukāḥ
c ṛṣer bhītāś ca śīghraṃ tu gamanāya matiṃ dadhuḥ
a asmākam api mukhyāni phalānīmāni vai dvija
c gṛhāṇa prati bhadraṃ te bhakṣayasva ca mā ciram
a tatas tās taṃ samāliṅgya sarvā harṣasamanvitāḥ
c modakān pradadus tasmai bhakṣyāṃś ca vividhāñ śubhān
a tāni cāsvādya tejasvī phalānīti sma manyate
c anāsvāditapūrvāṇi vane nityanivāsinām
a āpṛcchya ca tadā vipraṃ vratacaryāṃ nivedya ca
c gacchanti smāpadeśāt tā bhītās tasya pituḥ striyaḥ
a gatāsu tāsu sarvāsu kāśyapasyātmajo dvijaḥ
c asvasthahṛdayaś cāsīd duḥkhaṃ sma parivartate
a tato 'paredyus taṃ deśam ājagāma sa vīryavān
c manojñā yatra tā dṛṣṭā vāramukhyāḥ svalaṃkṛtāḥ
a dṛṣṭvaiva ca tadā vipram āyāntaṃ hṛṣṭa mānasāḥ
c upasṛtya tataḥ sarvās tās tam ūcur idaṃ vacaḥ
a ehy āśramapadaṃ saumya asmākam iti cābruvan
c tatrāpy eṣa vidhiḥ śrīmān viśeṣeṇa bhaviṣyati
a śrutvā tu vacanaṃ tāsāṃ sarvāsāṃ hṛdayaṃgamam
c gamanāya matiṃ cakre taṃ ca ninyus tadā striyaḥ
a tatra cānīyamāne tu vipre tasmin mahātmani
c vavarṣa sahasā devo jagat prahlādayaṃs tadā
a varṣeṇaivāgataṃ vipraṃ viṣayaṃ svaṃ narādhipaḥ
c pratyudgamya muniṃ prahvaḥ śirasā ca mahīṃ gataḥ
a arghyaṃ ca pradadau tasmai nyāyataḥ susamāhitaḥ
c vavre prasādaṃ viprendrān mā vipraṃ manyur āviśet
a antaḥpuraṃ praviśyāsmai kanyāṃ dattvā yathāvidhi
c śāntāṃ śāntena manasā rājā harṣam avāpa saḥ
a evaṃ sa nyavasat tatra sarvakāmaiḥ supūjitaḥ
c ṛṣyaśṛṅgo mahātejāḥ śāntayā saha bhāryayā
a bhūya eva ca rājendra śṛṇu me vacanaṃ hitam
c yathā sa devapravaraḥ kathayām āsa buddhimān
a ikṣvākūṇāṃ kule jāto bhaviṣyati sudhārmikaḥ
c rājā daśaratho nāmnā śrīmān satyapratiśravaḥ
a aṅgarājena sakhyaṃ ca tasya rājño bhaviṣyati
c kanyā cāsya mahābhāgā śāntā nāma bhaviṣyati
a putras tv aṅgasya rājñas tu romapāda iti śrutaḥ
c taṃ sa rājā daśaratho gamiṣyati mahāyaśāḥ
a anapatyo 'smi dharmātmañ śāntā bhāryā mama kratum
c āhareta tvayājñaptaḥ saṃtānārthaṃ kulasya ca
a śrutvā rājño 'tha tad vākyaṃ manasā sa vicintya ca
c pradāsyate putravantaṃ śāntā bhartāram ātmavān
a pratigṛhya ca taṃ vipraṃ sa rājā vigatajvaraḥ
c āhariṣyati taṃ yajñaṃ prahṛṣṭenāntarātmanā
a taṃ ca rājā daśaratho yaṣṭukāmaḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ
c ṛṣyaśṛṅgaṃ dvijaśreṣṭhaṃ varayiṣyati dharmavit
a yajñārthaṃ prasavārthaṃ ca svargārthaṃ ca nareśvaraḥ
c labhate ca sa taṃ kāmaṃ dvija mukhyād viśāṃ patiḥ
a putrāś cāsya bhaviṣyanti catvāro 'mitavikramāḥ
c vaṃśapratiṣṭhānakarāḥ sarvalokeṣu viśrutāḥ
a evaṃ sa devapravaraḥ pūrvaṃ kathitavān kathām
c sanatkumāro bhagavān purā devayuge prabhuḥ
a sa tvaṃ puruṣaśārdūla tam ānaya susatkṛtam
c svayam eva mahārāja gatvā sabalavāhanaḥ
a anumānya vasiṣṭhaṃ ca sūtavākyaṃ niśamya ca
c sāntaḥpuraḥ sahāmātyaḥ prayayau yatra sa dvijaḥ
a vanāni saritaś caiva vyatikramya śanaiḥ śanaiḥ
c abhicakrāma taṃ deśaṃ yatra vai munipuṃgavaḥ
a āsādya taṃ dvijaśreṣṭhaṃ romapādasamīpagam
c ṛṣiputraṃ dadarśādau dīpyamānam ivānalam
a tato rājā yathānyāyaṃ pūjāṃ cakre viśeṣataḥ
c sakhitvāt tasya vai rājñaḥ prahṛṣṭenāntarātmanā
a romapādena cākhyātam ṛṣiputrāya dhīmate
c sakhyaṃ saṃbandhakaṃ caiva tadā taṃ pratyapūjayat
a evaṃ susatkṛtas tena sahoṣitvā nararṣabhaḥ
c saptāṣṭadivasān rājā rājānam idam abravīt
a śāntā tava sutā rājan saha bhartrā viśāmpate
c madīyaṃ nagaraṃ yātu kāryaṃ hi mahad udyatam
a tatheti rājā saṃśrutya gamanaṃ tasya dhīmataḥ
c uvāca vacanaṃ vipraṃ gaccha tvaṃ saha bhāryayā
a ṛṣiputraḥ pratiśrutya tathety āha nṛpaṃ tadā
c sa nṛpeṇābhyanujñātaḥ prayayau saha bhāryayā
a tāv anyonyāñjaliṃ kṛtvā snehāt saṃśliṣya corasā
c nanandatur daśaratho romapādaś ca vīryavān
a tataḥ suhṛdam āpṛcchya prasthito raghunandanaḥ
c paurebhyaḥ preṣayām āsa dūtān vai śīghragāminaḥ
e kriyatāṃ nagaraṃ sarvaṃ kṣipram eva svalaṃkṛtam
a tataḥ prahṛṣṭāḥ paurās te śrutvā rājānam āgatam
c tathā pracakrus tat sarvaṃ rājñā yat preṣitaṃ tadā
a tataḥ svalaṃkṛtaṃ rājā nagaraṃ praviveśa ha
c śaṅkhadundubhinirghoṣaiḥ puraskṛtya dvijarṣabham
a tataḥ pramuditāḥ sarve dṛṣṭvā vai nāgarā dvijam
c praveśyamānaṃ satkṛtya narendreṇendrakarmaṇā
a antaḥpuraṃ praveśyainaṃ pūjāṃ kṛtvā tu śāstrataḥ
c kṛtakṛtyaṃ tadātmānaṃ mene tasyopavāhanāt
a antaḥpurāṇi sarvāṇi śāntāṃ dṛṣṭvā tathāgatām
c saha bhartrā viśālākṣīṃ prītyānandam upāgaman
a pūjyamānā ca tābhiḥ sā rājñā caiva viśeṣataḥ
c uvāsa tatra sukhitā kaṃ cit kālaṃ saha dvijā
a tataḥ kāle bahutithe kasmiṃś cit sumanohare
c vasante samanuprāpte rājño yaṣṭuṃ mano 'bhavat
a tataḥ prasādya śirasā taṃ vipraṃ devavarṇinam
c yajñāya varayām āsa saṃtānārthaṃ kulasya ca
a tatheti ca sa rājānam uvāca ca susatkṛtaḥ
c saṃbhārāḥ saṃbhriyantāṃ te turagaś ca vimucyatām
a tato rājābravīd vākyaṃ sumantraṃ mantrisattamam
c sumantrāvāhaya kṣipram ṛtvijo brahmavādinaḥ
a tataḥ sumantras tvaritaṃ gatvā tvaritavikramaḥ
c samānayat sa tān viprān samastān vedapāragān
a suyajñaṃ vāmadevaṃ ca jābālim atha kāśyapam
c purohitaṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ ca ye cānye dvijasattamāḥ
a tān pūjayitvā dharmātmā rājā daśarathas tadā
c idaṃ dharmārthasahitaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ vacanam abravīt
a mama lālapyamānasya putrārthaṃ nāsti vai sukham
c tadarthaṃ hayamedhena yakṣyāmīti matir mama
a tad ahaṃ yaṣṭum icchāmi śāstradṛṣṭena karmaṇā
c ṛṣiputraprabhāvena kāmān prāpsyāmi cāpy aham
a tataḥ sādhv iti tad vākyaṃ brāhmaṇāḥ pratyapūjayan
c vasiṣṭhapramukhāḥ sarve pārthivasya mukhāc cyutam
a ṛṣyaśṛṅgapurogāś ca pratyūcur nṛpatiṃ tadā
c saṃbhārāḥ saṃbhriyantāṃ te turagaś ca vimucyatām
a sarvathā prāpyase putrāṃś caturo 'mitavikramān
c yasya te dhārmikī buddhir iyaṃ putrārtham āgatāḥ
a tataḥ prīto 'bhavad rājā śrutvā tad dvijabhāṣitam
c amātyāṃś cābravīd rājā harṣeṇedaṃ śubhākṣaram
a gurūṇāṃ vacanāc chīghraṃ saṃbhārāḥ saṃbhriyantu me
c samarthādhiṣṭhitaś cāśvaḥ sopādhyāyo vimucyatām
a sarayvāś cottare tīre yajñabhūmir vidhīyatām
c śāntayaś cābhivardhantāṃ yathākalpaṃ yathāvidhi
a śakyaḥ kartum ayaṃ yajñaḥ sarveṇāpi mahīkṣitā
c nāparādho bhavet kaṣṭo yady asmin kratusattame
a chidraṃ hi mṛgayante 'tra vidvāṃso brahmarākṣasāḥ
c vidhihīnasya yajñasya sadyaḥ kartā vinaśyati
a tad yathāvidhi pūrvaṃ me kratur eṣa samāpyate
c tathāvidhānaṃ kriyatāṃ samarthāḥ karaṇeṣv iha
a tatheti ca tataḥ sarve mantriṇaḥ pratyapūjayan
c pārthivendrasya tad vākyaṃ yathājñaptam akurvata
a tato dvijās te dharmajñam astuvan pārthivarṣabham
c anujñātās tataḥ sarve punar jagmur yathāgatam
a gatānāṃ tu dvijātīnāṃ mantriṇas tān narādhipaḥ
c visarjayitvā svaṃ veśma praviveśa mahā dyutiḥ
a punaḥ prāpte vasante tu pūrṇaḥ saṃvatsaro 'bhavat
c abhivādya vasiṣṭhaṃ ca nyāyataḥ pratipūjya ca
a abravīt praśritaṃ vākyaṃ prasavārthaṃ dvijottamam
c yajño me kriyatāṃ vipra yathoktaṃ munipuṃgava
a yathā na vighnaḥ kriyate yajñāṅgeṣu vidhīyatām
c bhavān snigdhaḥ suhṛn mahyaṃ guruś ca paramo bhavān
a voḍhavyo bhavatā caiva bhāro yajñasya codyataḥ
c tatheti ca sa rājānam abravīd dvijasattamaḥ
a kariṣye sarvam evaitad bhavatā yat samarthitam
c tato 'bravīd dvijān vṛddhān yajñakarmasu niṣṭhitān
a sthāpatye niṣṭhitāṃś caiva vṛddhān paramadhārmikān
c karmāntikāñ śilpakārān vardhakīn khanakān api
a gaṇakāñ śilpinaś caiva tathaiva naṭanartakān
c tathā śucīñ śāstravidaḥ puruṣān subahuśrutān
a yajñakarma samīhantāṃ bhavanto rājaśāsanāt
c iṣṭakā bahusāhasrī śīghram ānīyatām iti
a aupakāryāḥ kriyantāṃ ca rājñāṃ bahuguṇānvitāḥ
c brāhmaṇāvasathāś caiva kartavyāḥ śataśaḥ śubhāḥ
a bhakṣyānnapānair bahubhiḥ samupetāḥ suniṣṭhitāḥ
c tathā paurajanasyāpi kartavyā bahuvistarāḥ
a āvāsā bahubhakṣyā vai sarvakāmair upasthitāḥ
c tathā jānapadasyāpi janasya bahuśobhanam
a dātavyam annaṃ vidhivat satkṛtya na tu līlayā
c sarvavarṇā yathā pūjāṃ prāpnuvanti susatkṛtāḥ
a na cāvajñā prayoktavyā kāmakrodhavaśād api
c yajñakarmasu ye 'vyagrāḥ puruṣāḥ śilpinas tathā
a teṣām api viśeṣeṇa pūjā kāryā yathākramam
c yathā sarvaṃ suvihitaṃ na kiṃ cit parihīyate
a tathā bhavantaḥ kurvantu prītisnigdhena cetasā
c tataḥ sarve samāgamya vasiṣṭham idam abruvan
a yathoktaṃ tat kariṣyāmo na kiṃ cit parihāsyate
c tataḥ sumantram āhūya vasiṣṭho vākyam abravīt
a nimantrayasya nṛpatīn pṛthivyāṃ ye ca dhārmikāḥ
c brāhmaṇān kṣatriyān vaiśyāñ śūdrāṃś caiva sahasraśaḥ
a samānayasva satkṛtya sarvadeśeṣu mānavān
c mithilādhipatiṃ śūraṃ janakaṃ satyavikramam
a niṣṭhitaṃ sarvaśāstreṣu tathā vedeṣu niṣṭhitam
c tam ānaya mahābhāgaṃ svayam eva susatkṛtam
e pūrvasaṃbandhinaṃ jñātvā tataḥ pūrvaṃ bravīmi te
a tathā kāśipatiṃ snigdhaṃ satataṃ priyavādinam
c sadvṛttaṃ devasaṃkāśaṃ svayam evānayasva ha
a tathā kekayarājānaṃ vṛddhaṃ paramadhārmikam
c śvaśuraṃ rājasiṃhasya saputraṃ tam ihānaya
a aṅgeśvaraṃ mahābhāgaṃ romapādaṃ susatkṛtam
c vayasyaṃ rājasiṃhasya tam ānaya yaśasvinam
a prācīnān sindhusauvīrān saurāṣṭhreyāṃś ca pārthivān
c dākṣiṇātyān narendrāṃś ca samastān ānayasva ha
a santi snigdhāś ca ye cānye rājānaḥ pṛthivītale
c tān ānaya yathākṣipraṃ sānugān sahabāndhavān
a vasiṣṭhavākyaṃ tac chrutvā sumantras tvaritas tadā
c vyādiśat puruṣāṃs tatra rājñām ānayane śubhān
a svayam eva hi dharmātmā prayayau muniśāsanāt
c sumantras tvarito bhūtvā samānetuṃ mahīkṣitaḥ
a te ca karmāntikāḥ sarve vasiṣṭhāya ca dhīmate
c sarvaṃ nivedayanti sma yajñe yad upakalpitam
a tataḥ prīto dvijaśreṣṭhas tān sarvān punar abravīt
c avajñayā na dātavyaṃ kasya cil līlayāpi vā
e avajñayā kṛtaṃ hanyād dātāraṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ
a tataḥ kaiś cid ahorātrair upayātā mahīkṣitaḥ
c bahūni ratnāny ādāya rājño daśarathasya ha
a tato vasiṣṭhaḥ suprīto rājānam idam abravīt
c upayātā naravyāghra rājānas tava śāsanāt
a mayāpi satkṛtāḥ sarve yathārhaṃ rājasattamāḥ
c yajñiyaṃ ca kṛtaṃ rājan puruṣaiḥ susamāhitaiḥ
a niryātu ca bhavān yaṣṭuṃ yajñāyatanam antikāt
c sarvakāmair upahṛtair upetaṃ vai samantataḥ
a tathā vasiṣṭhavacanād ṛṣyaśṛṅgasya cobhayoḥ
c śubhe divasa nakṣatre niryāto jagatīpatiḥ
a tato vasiṣṭhapramukhāḥ sarva eva dvijottamāḥ
c ṛṣyaśṛṅgaṃ puraskṛtya yajñakarmārabhaṃs tadā
a atha saṃvatsare pūrṇe tasmin prāpte turaṅgame
c sarayvāś cottare tīre rājño yajño 'bhyavartata
a ṛṣyaśṛṅgaṃ puraskṛtya karma cakrur dvijarṣabhāḥ
c aśvamedhe mahāyajñe rājño 'sya sumahātmanaḥ
a karma kurvanti vidhivad yājakā vedapāragāḥ
c yathāvidhi yathānyāyaṃ parikrāmanti śāstrataḥ
a pravargyaṃ śāstrataḥ kṛtvā tathaivopasadaṃ dvijāḥ
c cakruś ca vidhivat sarvam adhikaṃ karma śāstrataḥ
a abhipūjya tato hṛṣṭāḥ sarve cakrur yathāvidhi
c prātaḥsavanapūrvāṇi karmāṇi munipuṃgavāḥ
a na cāhutam abhūt tatra skhalitaṃ vāpi kiṃ cana
c dṛśyate brahmavat sarvaṃ kṣemayuktaṃ hi cakrire
a na teṣv ahaḥsu śrānto vā kṣudhito vāpi dṛśyate
c nāvidvān brāhmaṇas tatra nāśatānucaras tathā
a brāhmaṇā bhuñjate nityaṃ nāthavantaś ca bhuñjate
c tāpasā bhujate cāpi śramaṇā bhuñjate tathā
a vṛddhāś ca vyādhitāś caiva striyo bālās tathaiva ca
c aniśaṃ bhuñjamānānāṃ na tṛptir upalabhyate
a dīyatāṃ dīyatām annaṃ vāsāṃsi vividhāni ca
c iti saṃcoditās tatra tathā cakrur anekaśaḥ
a annakūṭāś ca bahavo dṛśyante parvatopamāḥ
c divase divase tatra siddhasya vidhivat tadā
a annaṃ hi vidhivat svādu praśaṃsanti dvijarṣabhāḥ
c aho tṛptāḥ sma bhadraṃ te iti śuśrāva rāghavaḥ
a svalaṃkṛtāś ca puruṣā brāhmaṇān paryaveṣayan
c upāsate ca tān anye sumṛṣṭamaṇikuṇḍalāḥ
a karmāntare tadā viprā hetuvādān bahūn api
c prāhuḥ suvāgmino dhīrāḥ parasparajigīṣayā
a divase divase tatra saṃstare kuśalā dvijāḥ
c sarvakarmāṇi cakrus te yathāśāstraṃ pracoditāḥ
a nāṣaḍaṅgavid atrāsīn nāvrato nābahuśrutaḥ
c sadasyas tasya vai rājño nāvādakuśalo dvijaḥ
a prāpte yūpocchraye tasmin ṣaḍ bailvāḥ khādirās tathā
c tāvanto bilvasahitāḥ parṇinaś ca tathāpare
a śleṣmātakamayo diṣṭo devadārumayas tathā
c dvāv eva tatra vihitau bāhuvyastaparigrahau
a kāritāḥ sarva evaite śāstrajñair yajñakovidaiḥ
c śobhārthaṃ tasya yajñasya kāñcanālaṃkṛtā bhavan
a vinyastā vidhivat sarve śilpibhiḥ sukṛtā dṛḍhāḥ
c aṣṭāśrayaḥ sarva eva ślakṣṇarūpasamanvitāḥ
a ācchāditās te vāsobhiḥ puṣpair gandhaiś ca bhūṣitāḥ
c saptarṣayo dīptimanto virājante yathā divi
a iṣṭakāś ca yathānyāyaṃ kāritāś ca pramāṇataḥ
c cito 'gnir brāhmaṇais tatra kuśalaiḥ śulbakarmaṇi
e sa cityo rājasiṃhasya saṃcitaḥ kuśalair dvijaiḥ
a garuḍo rukmapakṣo vai triguṇo 'ṣṭādaśātmakaḥ
c niyuktās tatra paśavas tat tad uddiśya daivatam
a uragāḥ pakṣiṇaś caiva yathāśāstraṃ pracoditāḥ
c śāmitre tu hayas tatra tathā jala carāś ca ye
a ṛtvigbhiḥ sarvam evaitan niyuktaṃ śāstratas tadā
c paśūnāṃ triśataṃ tatra yūpeṣu niyataṃ tadā
e aśvaratnottamaṃ tasya rājño daśarathasya ha
a kausalyā taṃ hayaṃ tatra paricarya samantataḥ
c kṛpāṇair viśaśāsainaṃ tribhiḥ paramayā mudā
a patatriṇā tadā sārdhaṃ susthitena ca cetasā
c avasad rajanīm ekāṃ kausalyā dharmakāmyayā
a hotādhvaryus tathodgātā hayena samayojayan
c mahiṣyā parivṛtthyātha vāvātām aparāṃ tathā
a patatriṇas tasya vapām uddhṛtya niyatendriyaḥ
c ṛtvik parama saṃpannaḥ śrapayām āsa śāstrataḥ
a dhūmagandhaṃ vapāyās tu jighrati sma narādhipaḥ
c yathākālaṃ yathānyāyaṃ nirṇudan pāpam ātmanaḥ
a hayasya yāni cāṅgāni tāni sarvāṇi brāhmaṇāḥ
c agnau prāsyanti vidhivat samastāḥ ṣoḍaśartvijaḥ
a plakṣaśākhāsu yajñānām anyeṣāṃ kriyate haviḥ
c aśvamedhasya caikasya vaitaso bhāga iṣyate
a tryaho 'śvamedhaḥ saṃkhyātaḥ kalpasūtreṇa brāhmaṇaiḥ
c catuṣṭomam ahas tasya prathamaṃ parikalpitam
a ukthyaṃ dvitīyaṃ saṃkhyātam atirātraṃ tathottaram
c kāritās tatra bahavo vihitāḥ śāstradarśanāt
a jyotiṣṭomāyuṣī caiva atirātrau ca nirmitau
c abhijid viśvajic caiva aptoryāmo mahākratuḥ
a prācīṃ hotre dadau rājā diśaṃ svakulavardhanaḥ
c adhvaryave pratīcīṃ tu brahmaṇe dakṣiṇāṃ diśam
a udgātre tu tathodīcīṃ dakṣiṇaiṣā vinirmitā
c aśvamedhe mahāyajñe svayambhuvihite purā
a kratuṃ samāpya tu tadā nyāyataḥ puruṣarṣabhaḥ
c ṛtvigbhyo hi dadau rājā dharāṃ tāṃ kratuvardhanaḥ
a ṛtvijas tv abruvan sarve rājānaṃ gatakalmaṣam
c bhavān eva mahīṃ kṛtsnām eko rakṣitum arhati
a na bhūmyā kāryam asmākaṃ na hi śaktāḥ sma pālane
c ratāḥ svādhyāyakaraṇe vayaṃ nityaṃ hi bhūmipa
e niṣkrayaṃ kiṃ cid eveha prayacchatu bhavān iti
a gavāṃ śatasahasrāṇi daśa tebhyo dadau nṛpaḥ
c daśakoṭiṃ suvarṇasya rajatasya caturguṇam
a ṛtvijas tu tataḥ sarve pradaduḥ sahitā vasu
c ṛṣyaśṛṅgāya munaye vasiṣṭhāya ca dhīmate
a tatas te nyāyataḥ kṛtvā pravibhāgaṃ dvijottamāḥ
c suprītamanasaḥ sarve pratyūcur muditā bhṛśam
a tataḥ prītamanā rājā prāpya yajñam anuttamam
c pāpāpahaṃ svarnayanaṃ dustaraṃ pārthivarṣabhaiḥ
a tato 'bravīd ṛṣyaśṛṅgaṃ rājā daśarathas tadā
c kulasya vardhanaṃ tat tu kartum arhasi suvrata
a tatheti ca sa rājānam uvāca dvijasattamaḥ
c bhaviṣyanti sutā rājaṃś catvāras te kulodvahāḥ
a medhāvī tu tato dhyātvā sa kiṃ cid idam uttamam
c labdhasaṃjñas tatas taṃ tu vedajño nṛpam abravīt
a iṣṭiṃ te 'haṃ kariṣyāmi putrīyāṃ putrakāraṇāt
c atharvaśirasi proktair mantraiḥ siddhāṃ vidhānataḥ
a tataḥ prākramad iṣṭiṃ tāṃ putrīyāṃ putra kāraṇāt
c juhāva cāgnau tejasvī mantradṛṣṭena karmaṇā
a tato devāḥ sagandharvāḥ siddhāś ca paramarṣayaḥ
c bhāgapratigrahārthaṃ vai samavetā yathāvidhi
a tāḥ sametya yathānyāyaṃ tasmin sadasi devatāḥ
c abruvaṃl lokakartāraṃ brahmāṇaṃ vacanaṃ mahat
a bhagavaṃs tvatprasādena rāvaṇo nāma rākṣasaḥ
c sarvānno bādhate vīryāc chāsituṃ taṃ na śaknumaḥ
a tvayā tasmai varo dattaḥ prītena bhagavan purā
c mānayantaś ca taṃ nityaṃ sarvaṃ tasya kṣamāmahe
a udvejayati lokāṃs trīn ucchritān dveṣṭi durmatiḥ
c śakraṃ tridaśarājānaṃ pradharṣayitum icchati
a ṛṣīn yakṣān sagandharvān asurān brāhmaṇāṃs tathā
c atikrāmati durdharṣo varadānena mohitaḥ
a nainaṃ sūryaḥ pratapati pārśve vāti na mārutaḥ
c calormimālī taṃ dṛṣṭvā samudro 'pi na kampate
a tan manan no bhayaṃ tasmād rākṣasād ghoradarśanāt
c vadhārthaṃ tasya bhagavann upāyaṃ kartum arhasi
a evam uktaḥ suraiḥ sarvaiś cintayitvā tato 'bravīt
c hantāyaṃ vihitas tasya vadhopāyo durātmanaḥ
a tena gandharvayakṣāṇāṃ devadānavarakṣasām
c avadhyo 'smīti vāg uktā tathety uktaṃ ca tan mayā
a nākīrtayad avajñānāt tad rakṣo mānuṣāṃs tadā
c tasmāt sa mānuṣād vadhyo mṛtur nānyo 'sya vidyate
a etac chrutvā priyaṃ vākyaṃ brahmaṇā samudāhṛtam
c devā maharṣayaḥ sarve prahṛṣṭās te 'bhavaṃs tadā
a etasminn antare viṣṇur upayāto mahādyutiḥ
c brahmaṇā ca samāgamya tatra tasthau samāhitaḥ
a tam abruvan surāḥ sarve samabhiṣṭūya saṃnatāḥ
c tvāṃ niyokṣyāmahe viṣṇo lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā
a rājño daśarathasya tvam ayodhyādhipater vibho
c dharmajñasya vadānyasya maharṣisamatejasaḥ
e tasya bhāryāsu tisṛṣu hrīśrīkīrtyupamāsu ca
g viṣṇo putratvam āgaccha kṛtvātmānaṃ caturvidham
a tatra tvaṃ mānuṣo bhūtvā pravṛddhaṃ lokakaṇṭakam
c avadhyaṃ daivatair viṣṇo samare jahi rāvaṇam
a sa hi devān sagandharvān siddhāṃś ca ṛṣisattamān
c rākṣaso rāvaṇo mūrkho vīryotsekena bādhate
a tad uddhataṃ rāvaṇam ṛddhatejasaṃ
pravṛddhadarpaṃ tridaśeśvaradviṣam
c virāvaṇaṃ sādhu tapasvikaṇṭakaṃ
tapasvinām uddhara taṃ bhayāvaham
a tato nārāyaṇo viṣṇur niyuktaḥ surasattamaiḥ
c jānann api surān evaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ vacanam abravīt
a upāyaḥ ko vadhe tasya rākṣasādhipateḥ surāḥ
c yam ahaṃ taṃ samāsthāya nihanyām ṛṣikaṇṭakam
a evam uktāḥ surāḥ sarve pratyūcur viṣṇum avyayam
c mānuṣīṃ tanum āsthāya rāvaṇaṃ jahi saṃyuge
a sa hi tepe tapas tīvraṃ dīrghakālam ariṃdama
c yena tuṣṭo 'bhavad brahmā lokakṛl lokapūjitaḥ
a saṃtuṣṭaḥ pradadau tasmai rākṣasāya varaṃ prabhuḥ
c nānāvidhebhyo bhūtebhyo bhayaṃ nānyatra mānuṣāt
a avajñātāḥ purā tena varadānena mānavāḥ
c tasmāt tasya vadho dṛṣṭo mānuṣebhyaḥ paraṃtapa
a ity etad vacanaṃ śrutvā surāṇāṃ viṣṇur ātmavān
c pitaraṃ rocayām āsa tadā daśarathaṃ nṛpam
a sa cāpy aputro nṛpatis tasmin kāle mahādyutiḥ
c ayajat putriyām iṣṭiṃ putrepsur arisūdanaḥ
a tato vai yajamānasya pāvakād atulaprabham
c prādurbhūtaṃ mahad bhūtaṃ mahāvīryaṃ mahābalam
a kṛṣṇaṃ raktāmbaradharaṃ raktāsyaṃ dundubhisvanam
c snigdhaharyakṣatanujaśmaśrupravaramūrdhajam
a śubhalakṣaṇasaṃpannaṃ divyābharaṇabhūṣitam
c śailaśṛṅgasamutsedhaṃ dṛptaśārdūlavikramam
a divākarasamākāraṃ dīptānalaśikhopamam
c taptajāmbūnadamayīṃ rājatāntaparicchadām
a divyapāyasasaṃpūrṇāṃ pātrīṃ patnīm iva priyām
c pragṛhya vipulāṃ dorbhyāṃ svayaṃ māyāmayīm iva
a samavekṣyābravīd vākyam idaṃ daśarathaṃ nṛpam
c prājāpatyaṃ naraṃ viddhi mām ihābhyāgataṃ nṛpa
a tataḥ paraṃ tadā rājā pratyuvāca kṛtāñjaliḥ
c bhagavan svāgataṃ te 'stu kim ahaṃ karavāṇi te
a atho punar idaṃ vākyaṃ prājāpatyo naro 'bravīt
c rājann arcayatā devān adya prāptam idaṃ tvayā
a idaṃ tu naraśārdūla pāyasaṃ devanirmitam
c prajākaraṃ gṛhāṇa tvaṃ dhanyam ārogyavardhanam
a bhāryāṇām anurūpāṇām aśnīteti prayaccha vai
c tāsu tvaṃ lapsyase putrān yadarthaṃ yajase nṛpa
a tatheti nṛpatiḥ prītaḥ śirasā pratigṛhyatām
c pātrīṃ devānnasaṃpūrṇāṃ devadattāṃ hiraṇmayīm
a abhivādya ca tad bhūtam adbhutaṃ priyadarśanam
c mudā paramayā yuktaś cakārābhipradakṣiṇam
a tato daśarathaḥ prāpya pāyasaṃ devanirmitam
c babhūva paramaprītaḥ prāpya vittam ivādhanaḥ
a tatas tad adbhutaprakhyaṃ bhūtaṃ paramabhāsvaram
c saṃvartayitvā tat karma tatraivāntaradhīyata
a harṣaraśmibhir udyotaṃ tasyāntaḥpuram ābabhau
c śāradasyābhirāmasya candrasyeva nabho'ṃśubhiḥ
a so 'ntaḥpuraṃ praviśyaiva kausalyām idam abravīt
c pāyasaṃ pratigṛhṇīṣva putrīyaṃ tv idam ātmanaḥ
a kausalyāyai narapatiḥ pāyasārdhaṃ dadau tadā
c ardhād ardhaṃ dadau cāpi sumitrāyai narādhipaḥ
a kaikeyyai cāvaśiṣṭārdhaṃ dadau putrārthakāraṇāt
c pradadau cāvaśiṣṭārdhaṃ pāyasasyāmṛtopamam
a anucintya sumitrāyai punar eva mahīpatiḥ
c evaṃ tāsāṃ dadau rājā bhāryāṇāṃ pāyasaṃ pṛthak
a tās tv etat pāyasaṃ prāpya narendrasyottamāḥ striyaḥ
c saṃmānaṃ menire sarvāḥ praharṣoditacetasaḥ
a putratvaṃ tu gate viṣṇau rājñas tasya mahātmanaḥ
c uvāca devatāḥ sarvāḥ svayambhūr bhagavān idam
a satyasaṃdhasya vīrasya sarveṣāṃ no hitaiṣiṇaḥ
c viṣṇoḥ sahāyān balinaḥ sṛjadhvaṃ kāmarūpiṇaḥ
a māyāvidaś ca śūrāṃś ca vāyuvegasamāñjave
c nayajñān buddhisaṃpannān viṣṇutulyaparākramān
a asaṃhāryān upāyajñān divyasaṃhananānvitān
c sarvāstraguṇasaṃpannān amṛtaprāśanān iva
a apsaraḥsu ca mukhyāsu gandharvīṇāṃ tanūṣu ca
c yakṣapannagakanyāsu ṛṣkavidyādharīṣu ca
a kiṃnarīṇāṃ ca gātreṣu vānarīṇāṃ tanūṣu ca
c sṛjadhvaṃ harirūpeṇa putrāṃs tulyaparākramān
a te tathoktā bhagavatā tat pratiśrutya śāsanam
c janayām āsur evaṃ te putrān vānararūpiṇaḥ
a ṛṣayaś ca mahātmānaḥ siddhavidyādharoragāḥ
c cāraṇāś ca sutān vīrān sasṛjur vanacāriṇaḥ
a te sṛṣṭā bahusāhasrā daśagrīvavadhodyatāḥ
c aprameyabalā vīrā vikrāntāḥ kāmarūpiṇaḥ
a te gajācalasaṃkāśā vapuṣmanto mahābalāḥ
c ṛkṣavānaragopucchāḥ kṣipram evābhijajñire
a yasya devasya yad rūpaṃ veṣo yaś ca parākramaḥ
c ajāyata samastena tasya tasya sutaḥ pṛthak
a golāṅgūlīṣu cotpannāḥ ke cit saṃmatavikramāḥ
c ṛkṣīṣu ca tathā jātā vānarāḥ kiṃnarīṣu ca
a śilāpraharaṇāḥ sarve sarve pādapayodhinaḥ
c nakhadaṃṣṭrāyudhāḥ sarve sarve sarvāstrakovidāḥ
a vicālayeyuḥ śailendrān bhedayeyuḥ sthirān drumān
c kṣobhayeyuś ca vegena samudraṃ saritāṃ patim
a dārayeyuḥ kṣitiṃ padbhyām āplaveyur mahārṇavam
c nabhastalaṃ viśeyuś ca gṛhṇīyur api toyadān
a gṛhṇīyur api mātaṅgān mattān pravrajato vane
c nardamānāṃś ca nādena pātayeyur vihaṃgamān
a īdṛśānāṃ prasūtāni harīṇāṃ kāmarūpimām
c śataṃ śatasahasrāṇi yūthapānāṃ mahātmanām
e babhūvur yūthapaśreṣṭhā vīrāṃś cājanayan harīn
a anye ṛkṣavataḥ prasthān upatasthuḥ sahasraśaḥ
c anye nānāvidhāñ śailān kānanāni ca bhejire
a sūryaputraṃ ca sugrīvaṃ śakraputraṃ ca vālinam
c bhrātarāv upatasthus te sarva eva harīśvarāḥ
a tair meghavṛndācalatulyakāyair
mahābalair vānarayūthapālaiḥ
c babhūva bhūr bhīmaśarīrarūpaiḥ
samāvṛtā rāmasahāyahetoḥ
a nirvṛtte tu kratau tasmin hayamedhe mahātmanaḥ
c pratigṛhya surā bhāgān pratijagmur yathāgatam
a samāptadīkṣāniyamaḥ patnīgaṇasamanvitaḥ
c praviveśa purīṃ rājā sabhṛtyabalavāhanaḥ
a yathārhaṃ pūjitās tena rājñā vai pṛthivīśvarāḥ
c muditāḥ prayayur deśān praṇamya munipuṃgavam
a gateṣu pṛthivīśeṣu rājā daśarathaḥ punaḥ
c praviveśa purīṃ śrīmān puraskṛtya dvijottamān
a śāntayā prayayau sārdham ṛṣyaśṛṅgaḥ supūjitaḥ
c anvīyamāno rājñātha sānuyātreṇa dhīmatā
a kausalyājanayad rāmaṃ divyalakṣaṇasaṃyutam
c viṣṇor ardhaṃ mahābhāgaṃ putram ikṣvākunandanam
a kausalyā śuśubhe tena putreṇāmitatejasā
c yathā vareṇa devānām aditir vajrapāṇinā
a bharato nāma kaikeyyāṃ jajñe satyaparākramaḥ
c sākṣād viṣṇoś caturbhāgaḥ sarvaiḥ samudito guṇaiḥ
a atha lakṣmaṇaśatrughnau sumitrājanayat sutau
c vīrau sarvāstrakuśalau viṣṇor ardhasamanvitau
a rājñaḥ putrā mahātmānaś catvāro jajñire pṛthak
c guṇavanto 'nurūpāś ca rucyā proṣṭhapadopamāḥ
a atītyaikādaśāhaṃ tu nāma karma tathākarot
c jyeṣṭhaṃ rāmaṃ mahātmānaṃ bharataṃ kaikayīsutam
a saumitriṃ lakṣmaṇam iti śatrughnam aparaṃ tathā
c vasiṣṭhaḥ paramaprīto nāmāni kṛtavāṃs tadā
e teṣāṃ janmakriyādīni sarvakarmāṇy akārayat
a teṣāṃ ketur iva jyeṣṭho rāmo ratikaraḥ pituḥ
c babhūva bhūyo bhūtānāṃ svayambhūr iva saṃmataḥ
a sarve vedavidaḥ śūrāḥ sarve lokahite ratāḥ
c sarve jñānopasaṃpannāḥ sarve samuditā guṇaiḥ
a teṣām api mahātejā rāmaḥ satyaparākramaḥ
c bālyāt prabhṛti susnigdho lakṣmaṇo lakṣmivardhanaḥ
a rāmasya lokarāmasya bhrātur jyeṣṭhasya nityaśaḥ
c sarvapriyakaras tasya rāmasyāpi śarīrataḥ
a lakṣmaṇo lakṣmisaṃpanno bahiḥprāṇa ivāparaḥ
c na ca tena vinā nidrāṃ labhate puruṣottamaḥ
e mṛṣṭam annam upānītam aśnāti na hi taṃ vinā
a yadā hi hayam ārūḍho mṛgayāṃ yāti rāghavaḥ
c tadainaṃ pṛṣṭhato 'bhyeti sadhanuḥ paripālayan
a bharatasyāpi śatrughno lakṣmaṇāvarajo hi saḥ
c prāṇaiḥ priyataro nityaṃ tasya cāsīt tathā priyaḥ
a sa caturbhir mahābhāgaiḥ putrair daśarathaḥ priyaiḥ
c babhūva paramaprīto devair iva pitāmahaḥ
a te yadā jñānasaṃpannāḥ sarve samuditā guṇaiḥ
c hrīmantaḥ kīrtimantaś ca sarvajñā dīrghadarśinaḥ
a atha rājā daśarathas teṣāṃ dārakriyāṃ prati
c cintayām āsa dharmātmā sopādhyāyaḥ sabāndhavaḥ
a tasya cintayamānasya mantrimadhye mahātmanaḥ
c abhyāgacchan mahātejo viśvāmitro mahāmuniḥ
a sa rājño darśanākāṅkṣī dvārādhyakṣān uvāca ha
c śīghram ākhyāta māṃ prāptaṃ kauśikaṃ gādhinaḥ sutam
a tac chrutvā vacanaṃ tasya rājaveśma pradudruvuḥ
c saṃbhrāntamanasaḥ sarve tena vākyena coditāḥ
a te gatvā rājabhavanaṃ viśvāmitram ṛṣiṃ tadā
c prāptam āvedayām āsur nṛpāyekṣvākave tadā
a teṣāṃ tad vacanaṃ śrutvā sapurodhāḥ samāhitaḥ
c pratyujjagāma saṃhṛṣṭo brahmāṇam iva vāsavaḥ
a sa dṛṣṭvā jvalitaṃ dīptyā tāpasaṃ saṃśitavratam
c prahṛṣṭavadano rājā tato 'rghyam upahārayat
a sa rājñaḥ pratigṛhyārghyaṃ śāstradṛṣṭtena karmaṇā
c kuśalaṃ cāvyayaṃ caiva paryapṛcchan narādhipam
a vasiṣṭhaṃ ca samāgamya kuśalaṃ munipuṃgavaḥ
c ṛṣīṃś ca tān yathā nyāyaṃ mahābhāgān uvāca ha
a te sarve hṛṣṭamanasas tasya rājño niveśanam
c viviśuḥ pūjitās tatra niṣeduś ca yathārthataḥ
a atha hṛṣṭamanā rājā viśvāmitraṃ mahāmunim
c uvāca paramodāro hṛṣṭas tam abhipūjayan
a yathāmṛtasya saṃprāptir yathā varṣam anūdake
c yathā sadṛśadāreṣu putrajanmāprajasya ca
e pranaṣṭasya yathā lābho yathā harṣo mahodaye
g tathaivāgamanaṃ manye svāgataṃ te mahāmune
a kaṃ ca te paramaṃ kāmaṃ karomi kim u harṣitaḥ
c pātrabhūto 'si me vipra diṣṭyā prāpto 'si dhārmika
e adya me saphalaṃ janma jīvitaṃ ca sujīvitam
a pūrvaṃ rājarṣiśabdena tapasā dyotitaprabhaḥ
c brahmarṣitvam anuprāptaḥ pūjyo 'si bahudhā mayā
a tad adbhutam idaṃ vipra pavitraṃ paramaṃ mama
c śubhakṣetragataś cāhaṃ tava saṃdarśanāt prabho
a brūhi yat prārthitaṃ tubhyaṃ kāryam āgamanaṃ prati
c icchāmy anugṛhīto 'haṃ tvadarthaparivṛddhaye
a kāryasya na vimarśaṃ ca gantum arhasi kauśika
c kartā cāham aśeṣeṇa daivataṃ hi bhavān mama
a iti hṛdayasukhaṃ niśamya vākyaṃ
śrutisukham ātmavatā vinītam uktam
c prathitaguṇayaśā guṇair viśiṣṭaḥ
parama ṛṣiḥ paramaṃ jagāma harṣam
a tac chrutvā rājasiṃhasya vākyam adbhutavistaram
c hṛṣṭaromā mahātejā viśvāmitro 'bhyabhāṣata
a sadṛśaṃ rājaśārdūla tavaitad bhuvi nānyataḥ
c mahāvaṃśaprasūtasya vasiṣṭhavyapadeśinaḥ
a yat tu me hṛdgataṃ vākyaṃ tasya kāryasya niścayam
c kuruṣva rājaśārdūla bhava satyapratiśravaḥ
a ahaṃ niyamam ātiṣṭha siddhyarthaṃ puruṣarṣabha
c tasya vighnakarau dvau tu rākṣasau kāmarūpiṇau
a vrate me bahuśaś cīrṇe samāptyāṃ rākṣasāv imau
c mārīcaś ca subāhuś ca vīryavantau suśikṣitau
e tau māṃsarudhiraugheṇa vediṃ tām abhyavarṣatām
a avadhūte tathā bhūte tasmin niyamaniścaye
c kṛtaśramo nirutsāhas tasmād deśād apākrame
a na ca me krodham utsraṣṭuṃ buddhir bhavati pārthiva
c tathābhūtā hi sā caryā na śāpas tatra mucyate
a svaputraṃ rājaśārdūla rāmaṃ satyaparākramam
c kākapakṣadharaṃ śūraṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ me dātum arhasi
a śakto hy eṣa mayā gupto divyena svena tejasā
c rākṣasā ye vikartāras teṣām api vināśane
a śreyaś cāsmai pradāsyāmi bahurūpaṃ na saṃśayaḥ
c trayāṇām api lokānāṃ yena khyātiṃ gamiṣyati
a na ca tau rāmam āsādya śaktau sthātuṃ kathaṃ cana
c na ca tau rāghavād anyo hantum utsahate pumān
a vīryotsiktau hi tau pāpau kālapāśavaśaṃ gatau
c rāmasya rājaśārdūla na paryāptau mahātmanaḥ
a na ca putrakṛtaṃ snehaṃ kartum arhasi pārthiva
c ahaṃ te pratijānāmi hatau tau viddhi rākṣasau
a ahaṃ vedmi mahātmānaṃ rāmaṃ satyaparākramam
c vasiṣṭho 'pi mahātejā ye ceme tapasi sthitāḥ
a yadi te dharmalābhaṃ ca yaśaś ca paramaṃ bhuvi
c sthiram icchasi rājendra rāmaṃ me dātum arhasi
a yady abhyanujñāṃ kākutstha dadate tava mantriṇaḥ
c vasiṣṭha pramukhāḥ sarve tato rāmaṃ visarjaya
a abhipretam asaṃsaktam ātmajaṃ dātum arhasi
c daśarātraṃ hi yajñasya rāmaṃ rājīvalocanam
a nātyeti kālo yajñasya yathāyaṃ mama rāghava
c tathā kuruṣva bhadraṃ te mā ca śoke manaḥ kṛthāḥ
a ity evam uktvā dharmātmā dharmārthasahitaṃ vacaḥ
c virarāma mahātejā viśvāmitro mahāmuniḥ
a iti hṛdayamanovidāraṇaṃ
munivacanaṃ tad atīva śuśruvān
c narapatir agamad bhayaṃ mahad
vyathitamanāḥ pracacāla cāsanāt
a tac chrutvā rājaśārdūla viśvāmitrasya bhāṣitam
c muhūrtam iva niḥsaṃjñaḥ saṃjñāvān idam abravīt
a ūnaṣoḍaśavarṣo me rāmo rājīvalocanaḥ
c na yuddhayogyatām asya paśyāmi saha rākṣasaiḥ
a iyam akṣauhiṇī pūrṇā yasyāhaṃ patir īśvaraḥ
c anayā saṃvṛto gatvā yodhāhaṃ tair niśācaraiḥ
a ime śūrāś ca vikrāntā bhṛtyā me 'straviśāradāḥ
c yogyā rakṣogaṇair yoddhuṃ na rāmaṃ netum arhasi
a aham eva dhanuṣpāṇir goptā samaramūrdhani
c yāvat prāṇān dhariṣyāmi tāvad yotsye niśācaraiḥ
a nirvighnā vratavaryā sā bhaviṣyati surakṣitā
c ahaṃ tatra gamiṣyāmil na rāma netum arhasi
a bālo hy akṛtavidyaś ca na ca vetti balābalam
c na cāstrabalasaṃyukto na ca yuddhaviśāradaḥ
e na cāsau rakṣasāṃ yogyaḥ kūṭayuddhā hi te dhruvam
a viprayukto hi rāmeṇa muhūrtam api notsahe
c jīvituṃ muniśārdūla na rāmaṃ netum arhasi
a yadi vā rāghavaṃ brahman netum icchasi suvrata
c caturaṅgasamāyuktaṃ mayā saha ca taṃ naya
a ṣaṣṭir varṣasahasrāṇi jātasya mama kauśikaḥ
c duḥkhenotpāditaś cāyaṃ na rāmaṃ netum arhasi
a caturṇām ātmajānāṃ hi prītiḥ paramikā mama
c jyeṣṭhaṃ dharmapradhānaṃ ca na rāmaṃ netum arhasi
a kiṃ vīryā rākṣasās te ca kasya putrāś ca ke ca te
c kathaṃ pramāṇāḥ ke caitān rakṣanti munipuṃgava
a kathaṃ ca pratikartavyaṃ teṣāṃ rāmeṇa rakṣasām
c māmakair vā balair brahman mayā vā kūṭayodhinām
a sarvaṃ me śaṃsa bhagavan kathaṃ teṣāṃ mayā raṇe
c sthātavyaṃ duṣṭabhāvānāṃ vīryotsiktā hi rākṣasāḥ
a tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā viśvāmitro 'bhyabhāṣata
c paulastyavaṃśaprabhavo rāvaṇo nāma rākṣasaḥ
a sa brahmaṇā dattavaras trailokyaṃ bādhate bhṛśam
c mahābalo mahāvīryo rākṣasair bahubhir vṛtaḥ
a śrūyate hi mahāvīryo rāvaṇo rākṣasādhipaḥ
c sākṣād vaiśravaṇabhrātā putro viśvaraso muneḥ
a yadā svayaṃ na yajñasya vighnakartā mahābalaḥ
c tena saṃcoditau tau tu rākṣasau sumahā balau
e mārīcaś ca subāhuś ca yajñavighnaṃ kariṣyataḥ
a ity ukto muninā tena rājovāca muniṃ tadā
c na hi śakto 'smi saṃgrāme sthātuṃ tasya durātmanaḥ
a sa tvaṃ prasādaṃ dharmajña kuruṣva mama putrake
c devadānavagandharvā yakṣāḥ pataga pannagāḥ
a na śaktā rāvaṇaṃ soḍhuṃ kiṃ punar mānavā yudhi
c sa hi vīryavatāṃ vīryam ādatte yudhi rākṣasaḥ
a tena cāhaṃ na śakto 'smi saṃyoddhuṃ tasya vā balaiḥ
c sabalo vā muniśreṣṭha sahito vā mamātmajaiḥ
a katham apy amaraprakhyaṃ saṃgrāmāṇām akovidam
c bālaṃ me tanayaṃ brahman naiva dāsyāmi putrakam
a atha kālopamau yuddhe sutau sundopasundayoḥ
c yajñavighnakarau tau te naiva dāsyāmi putrakam
a mārīcaś ca subāhuś ca vīryavantau suśikṣitau
c tayor anyatareṇāhaṃ yoddhā syāṃ sasuhṛdgaṇaḥ
a tac chrutvā vacanaṃ tasya snehaparyākulākṣaram
c samanyuḥ kauśiko vākyaṃ pratyuvaca mahīpatim
a pūrvam arthaṃ pratiśrutya pratijñāṃ hātum icchasi
c rāgavāṇām ayukto 'yaṃ kulasyāsya viparyayaḥ
a yad idaṃ te kṣamaṃ rājan gamiṣyāmi yathāgatam
c mithyāpratijñaḥ kākutstha sukhī bhava sabāndhavaḥ
a tasya roṣaparītasya viśvāmitrasya dhīmataḥ
c cacāla vasudhā kṛtsnā viveśa ca bhayaṃ surān
a trastarūpaṃ tu vijñāya jagat sarvaṃ mahān ṛṣiḥ
c nṛpatiṃ suvrato dhīro vasiṣṭho vākyam abravīt
a ikṣvākūṇāṃ kule jātaḥ sākṣād dharma ivāparaḥ
c dhṛtimānsuvrataḥ śrīmān na dharmaṃ hātum arhasi
a triṣu lokeṣu vikhyāto dharmātmā iti rāghavaḥ
c svadharmaṃ pratipadyasva nādharmaṃ voḍhum arhasi
a saṃśrutyaivaṃ kariṣyāmīty akurvāṇasya rāghava
c iṣṭāpūrtavadho bhūyāt tasmād rāmaṃ visarjaya
a kṛtāstram akṛtāstraṃ vā nainaṃ śakṣyanti rākṣasāḥ
c guptaṃ kuśikaputreṇa jvalanenāmṛtaṃ yathā
a eṣa vigrahavān dharma eṣa vīryavatāṃ varaḥ
c eṣa buddhyādhiko loke tapasaś ca parāyaṇam
a eṣo 'strān vividhān vetti trailokye sacarācare
c nainam anyaḥ pumān vetti na ca vetsyanti ke cana
a na devā narṣayaḥ ke cin nāsurā na ca rākṣasāḥ
c gandharvayakṣapravarāḥ sakiṃnaramahoragāḥ
a sarvāstrāṇi kṛśāśvasya putrāḥ paramadhārmikāḥ
c kauśikāya purā dattā yadā rājyaṃ praśāsati
a te 'pi putrāḥ kṛśāśvasya prajāpatisutāsutāḥ
c nakarūpā mahāvīryā dīptimanto jayāvahāḥ
a jayā ca suprabhā caiva dakṣakanye sumadhyame
c te suvāte 'straśastrāṇi śataṃ parama bhāsvaram
a pañcāśataṃ sutāṃl lebhe jayā nāma varān purā
c vadhāyāsurasainyānām ameyān kāmarūpiṇaḥ
a suprabhājanayac cāpi putrān pañcāśataṃ punaḥ
c saṃhārān nāma durdharṣān durākrāmān balīyasaḥ
a tāni cāstrāṇi vetty eṣa yathāvat kuśikātmajaḥ
c apūrvāṇāṃ ca janane śakto bhūyaś ca dharmavit
a evaṃ vīryo mahātejā viśvāmitro mahātapāḥ
c na rāmagamane rājan saṃśayaṃ gantum arhasi
a tathā vasiṣṭhe bruvati rājā daśarathaḥ sutam
c prahṛṣṭavadano rāmam ājuhāva salakṣmaṇam
a kṛtasvastyayanaṃ mātrā pitrā daśarathena ca
c purodhasā vasiṣṭhena maṅgalair abhimantritam
a sa putraṃ mūrdhny upāghrāya rājā daśarathaḥ priyam
c dadau kuśikaputrāya suprītenāntarātmanā
a tato vāyuḥ sukhasparśo virajasko vavau tadā
c viśvāmitragataṃ rāmaṃ dṛṣṭvā rājīvalocanam
a puṣpavṛṣṭir mahaty āsīd devadundubhinisvanaḥ
c śaṅkhadundubhinirghoṣaḥ prayāte tu mahātmani
a viśvāmitro yayāv agre tato rāmo mahāyaśāḥ
c kākapakṣadharo dhanvī taṃ ca saumitrir anvagāt
a kalāpinau dhanuṣpāṇī śobhayānau diśo daśa
c viśvāmitraṃ mahātmānaṃ triśīrṣāv iva pannagau
e anujagmatur akṣudrau pitāmaham ivāśvinau
a baddhagodhāṅgulitrāṇau khaḍgavantau mahādyutī
c sthāṇuṃ devam ivācintyaṃ kumārāv iva pāvakī
a adhyardhayojanaṃ gatvā sarayvā dakṣiṇe taṭe
c rāmeti madhurā vāṇīṃ viśvāmitro 'bhyabhāṣata
a gṛhāṇa vatsa salilaṃ mā bhūt kālasya paryayaḥ
c mantragrāmaṃ gṛhāṇa tvaṃ balām atibalāṃ tathā
a na śramo na jvaro vā te na rūpasya viparyayaḥ
c na ca suptaṃ pramattaṃ vā dharṣayiṣyanti nairṛtāḥ
a na bāhvoḥ sadṛśo vīrye pṛthivyām asti kaś cana
c triṣu lokeṣu vā rāma na bhavet sadṛśas tava
a na saubhāgye na dākṣiṇye na jñāne buddhiniścaye
c nottare pratipattavyo samo loke tavānagha
a etadvidyādvaye labdhe bhavitā nāsti te samaḥ
c balā cātibalā caiva sarvajñānasya mātarau
a kṣutpipāse na te rāma bhaviṣyete narottama
c balām atibalāṃ caiva paṭhataḥ pathi rāghava
e vidyādvayam adhīyāne yaśaś cāpy atulaṃ bhuvi
a pitāmahasute hy ete vidye tejaḥsamanvite
c pradātuṃ tava kākutstha sadṛśas tvaṃ hi dhārmika
a kāmaṃ bahuguṇāḥ sarve tvayy ete nātra saṃśayaḥ
c tapasā saṃbhṛte caite bahurūpe bhaviṣyataḥ
a tato rāmo jalaṃ spṛṣṭvā prahṛṣṭavadanaḥ śuciḥ
c pratijagrāha te vidye maharṣer bhāvitātmanaḥ
e vidyāsamudito rāmaḥ śuśubhe bhūrivikramaḥ
a gurukāryāṇi sarvāṇi niyujya kuśikātmaje
c ūṣus tāṃ rajanīṃ tatra sarayvāṃ susukhaṃ trayaḥ
a prabhātāyāṃ tu śarvaryāṃ viśvāmitro mahāmuniḥ
c abhyabhāṣata kākutsthaṃ śayānaṃ parṇasaṃstare
a kausalyā suprajā rāma pūrvā saṃdhyā pravartate
c uttiṣṭha naraśārdūla kartavyaṃ daivam āhnikam
a tasyarṣeḥ paramodāraṃ vacaḥ śrutvā nṛpātmajau
c snātvā kṛtodakau vīrau jepatuḥ paramaṃ japam
a kṛtāhnikau mahāvīryau viśvāmitraṃ tapodhanam
c abhivādyābhisaṃhṛṣṭau gamanāyopatasthatuḥ
a tau prayāte mahāvīryau divyaṃ tripathagāṃ nadīm
c dadṛśāte tatas tatra sarayvāḥ saṃgame śubhe
a tatrāśramapadaṃ puṇyam ṛṣīṇām ugratejasām
c bahuvarṣasahasrāṇi tapyatāṃ paramaṃ tapaḥ
a taṃ dṛṣṭvā paramaprītau rāghavau puṇyam āśramam
c ūcatus taṃ mahātmānaṃ viśvāmitram idaṃ vacaḥ
a kasyāyam āśramaḥ puṇyaḥ ko nv asmin vasate pumān
c bhagavañ śrotum icchāvaḥ paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hi nau
a tayos tad vacanaṃ śrutvā prahasya munipuṃgavaḥ
c abravīc chrūyatāṃ rāma yasyāyaṃ pūrva āśramaḥ
a kandarpo mūrtimān āsīt kāma ity ucyate budhaiḥ
a tapasyantam iha sthāṇuṃ niyamena samāhitam
c kṛtodvāhaṃ tu deveśaṃ gacchantaṃ samarudgaṇam
e dharṣayām āsa durmedhā huṃkṛtaś ca mahātmanā
a dagdhasya tasya raudreṇa cakṣuṣā raghunandana
c vyaśīryanta śarīrāt svāt sarvagātrāṇi durmateḥ
a tasya gātraṃ hataṃ tatra nirdagdhasya mahātmanā
c aśarīraḥ kṛtaḥ kāmaḥ krodhād deveśvareṇa ha
a anaṅga iti vikhyātas tadā prabhṛti rāghava
c sa cāṅgaviṣayaḥ śrīmān yatrāṅgaṃ sa mumoca ha
a tasyāyam āśramaḥ puṇyas tasyeme munayaḥ purā
c śiṣyā dharmaparā vīra teṣāṃ pāpaṃ na vidyate
a ihādya rajanīṃ rāma vasema śubhadarśana
c puṇyayoḥ saritor madhye śvas tariṣyāmahe vayam
a teṣāṃ saṃvadatāṃ tatra tapo dīrgheṇa cakṣuṣā
c vijñāya paramaprītā munayo harṣam āgaman
a arghyaṃ pādyaṃ tathātithyaṃ nivedyakuśikātmaje
c rāmalakṣmaṇayoḥ paścād akurvann atithikriyām
a satkāraṃ samanuprāpya kathābhir abhirañjayan
c nyavasan susukhaṃ tatra kāmāśramapade tadā
a tataḥ prabhāte vimale kṛtāhnikam ariṃdamau
c viśvāmitraṃ puraskṛtya nadyās tīram upāgatau
a te ca sarve mahātmāno munayaḥ saṃśitavratāḥ
c upasthāpya śubhāṃ nāvaṃ viśvāmitram athābruvan
a ārohatu bhavān nāvaṃ rājaputrapuraskṛtaḥ
c ariṣṭaṃ gaccha panthānaṃ mā bhūt kālasya paryayaḥ
a viśvāmitras tathety uktvā tān ṛṣīn abhipūjya ca
c tatāra sahitas tābhyāṃ saritaṃ sāgaraṃ gamām
a atha rāmaḥ sarinmadhye papraccha munipuṅgavam
c vāriṇo bhidyamānasya kim ayaṃ tumulo dhvaniḥ
a rāghavasya vacaḥ śrutvā kautūhala samanvitam
c kathayām āsa dharmātmā tasya śabdasya niścayam
a kailāsaparvate rāma manasā nirmitaṃ saraḥ
c brahmaṇā naraśārdūla tenedaṃ mānasaṃ saraḥ
a tasmāt susrāva sarasaḥ sāyodhyām upagūhate
c saraḥpravṛttā sarayūḥ puṇyā brahmasaraścyutā
a tasyāyam atulaḥ śabdo jāhnavīm abhivartate
c vārisaṃkṣobhajo rāma praṇāmaṃ niyataḥ kuru
a tābhyāṃ tu tāv ubhau kṛtvā praṇāmam atidhārmikau
c tīraṃ dakṣiṇam āsādya jagmatur laghuvikramau
a sa vanaṃ ghorasaṃkāśaṃ dṛṣṭvā nṛpavarātmajaḥ
c aviprahatam aikṣvākaḥ papraccha munipuṃgavam
a aho vanam idaṃ durgaṃ jhillikāgaṇanāditam
c bhairavaiḥ śvāpadaiḥ kīrṇaṃ śakuntair dāruṇāravaiḥ
a nānāprakāraiḥ śakunair vāśyadbhir bhairavasvanaiḥ
c siṃhavyāghravarāhaiś ca vāraṇaiś cāpi śobhitam
a dhavāśvakarṇakakubhair bilvatindukapāṭalaiḥ
c saṃkīrṇaṃ badarībhiś ca kiṃ nv idaṃ dāruṇaṃ vanam
a tam uvāca mahātejā viśvāmitro mahāmuniḥ
c śrūyatāṃ vatsa kākutstha yasyaitad dāruṇaṃ vanam
a etau janapadau sphītau pūrvam āstāṃ narottama
c maladāś ca karūṣāś ca devanirmāṇa nirmitau
a purā vṛtravadhe rāma malena samabhiplutam
c kṣudhā caiva sahasrākṣaṃ brahmahatyā yadāviśat
a tam indraṃ snāpayan devā ṛṣayaś ca tapodhanāḥ
c kalaśaiḥ snāpayām āsur malaṃ cāsya pramocayan
a iha bhūmyāṃ malaṃ dattvā dattvā kāruṣam eva ca
c śarīrajaṃ mahendrasya tato harṣaṃ prapedire
a nirmalo niṣkarūṣaś ca śucir indro yadābhavat
c dadau deśasya suprīto varaṃ prabhur anuttamam
a imau janapadau sthītau khyātiṃ loke gamiṣyataḥ
c maladāś ca karūṣāś ca mamāṅgamaladhāriṇau
a sādhu sādhv iti taṃ devāḥ pākaśāsanam abruvan
c deśasya pūjāṃ tāṃ dṛṣṭvā kṛtāṃ śakreṇa dhīmatā
a etau janapadau sthītau dīrghakālam ariṃdama
c maladāś ca karūṣāś ca muditau dhanadhānyataḥ
a kasya cit tv atha kālasya yakṣī vai kāmarūpiṇī
c balaṃ nāgasahasrasya dhārayantī tadā hy abhūt
a tāṭakā nāma bhadraṃ te bhāryā sundasya dhīmataḥ
c mārīco rākṣasaḥ putro yasyāḥ śakraparākramaḥ
a imau janapadau nityaṃ vināśayati rāghava
c maladāṃś ca karūṣāṃś ca tāṭakā duṣṭacāriṇī
a seyaṃ panthānam āvārya vasaty atyardhayojane
c ata eva ca gantavyaṃ tāṭakāyā vanaṃ yataḥ
a svabāhubalam āśritya jahīmāṃ duṣṭacāriṇīm
c manniyogād imaṃ deśaṃ kuru niṣkaṇṭakaṃ punaḥ
a na hi kaś cid imaṃ deśaṃ śakroty āgantum īdṛśam
c yakṣiṇyā ghorayā rāma utsāditam asahyayā
a etat te sarvam ākhyātaṃ yathaitad daruṇaṃ vanam
c yakṣyā cotsāditaṃ sarvam adyāpi na nivartate
a atha tasyāprameyasya muner vacanam uttamam
c śrutvā puruṣaśārdūlaḥ pratyuvāca śubhāṃ giram
a alpavīryā yadā yakṣāḥ śrūyante munipuṃgava
c kathaṃ nāgasahasrasya dhārayaty abalā balam
a viśvāmitro 'bravīd vākyaṃ śṛṇu yena balottarā
c varadānakṛtaṃ vīryaṃ dhārayaty abalā balam
a pūrvam āsīn mahāyakṣaḥ suketur nāma vīryavān
c anapatyaḥ śubhācāraḥ sa ca tepe mahat tapaḥ
a pitāmahas tu suprītas tasya yakṣapates tadā
c kanyāratnaṃ dadau rāma tāṭakāṃ nāma nāmataḥ
a dadau nāgasahasrasya balaṃ cāsyāḥ pitāmahaḥ
c na tv eva putraṃ yakṣāya dadau brahmā mahāyaśāḥ
a tāṃ tu jātāṃ vivardhantīṃ rūpayauvanaśālinīm
c jambhaputrāya sundāya dadau bhāryāṃ yaśasvinīm
a kasya cit tv atha kālalsya yakṣī putraṃ vyajāyata
c mārīcaṃ nāma durdharṣaṃ yaḥ śāpād rākṣaso 'bhavat
a sunde tu nihate rāma agastyam ṛṣisattamam
c tāṭakā saha putreṇa pradharṣayitum icchati
a rākṣasatvaṃ bhajasveti mārīcaṃ vyājahāra saḥ
c agastyaḥ paramakruddhas tāṭakām api śaptavān
a puruṣādī mahāyakṣī virūpā vikṛtānanā
c idaṃ rūpam apahāya dāruṇaṃ rūpam astu te
a saiṣā śāpakṛtāmarṣā tāṭakā krodhamūrchitā
c deśam utsādayaty enam agastyacaritaṃ śubham
a enāṃ rāghava durvṛttāṃ yakṣīṃ paramadāruṇām
c gobrāhmaṇahitārthāya jahi duṣṭaparākramām
a na hy enāṃ śāpasaṃsṛṣṭāṃ kaś cid utsahate pumān
c nihantuṃ triṣu lokeṣu tvām ṛte raghunandana
a na hi te strīvadhakṛte ghṛṇā kāryā narottama
c cāturvarṇyahitārthāya kartavyaṃ rājasūnunā
a rājyabhāraniyuktānām eṣa dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ
c adharmyāṃ jahi kākutsha dharmo hy asyā na vidyate
a śrūyate hi purā śakro virocanasutāṃ nṛpa
c pṛthivīṃ hantum icchantīṃ mantharām abhyasūdayat
a viṣṇunā ca purā rāma bhṛgupatnī dṛḍhavratā
c anindraṃ lokam icchantī kāvyamātā niṣūditā
a etaiś cānyaiś ca bahubhī rājaputramahātmabhiḥ
c adharmaniratā nāryo hatāḥ puruṣasattamaiḥ
a muner vacanam aklībaṃ śrutvā naravarātmajaḥ
c rāghavaḥ prāñjalir bhūtvā pratyuvāca dṛḍhavrataḥ
a pitur vacananirdeśāt pitur vacanagauravāt
c vacanaṃ kauśikasyeti kartavyam aviśaṅkayā
a anuśiṣṭo 'smy ayodhyāyāṃ gurumadhye mahātmanā
c pitrā daśarathenāhaṃ nāvajñeyaṃ ca tad vacaḥ
a so 'haṃ pitur vacaḥ śrutvā śāsanād brahma vādinaḥ
c kariṣyāmi na saṃdehas tāṭakāvadham uttamam
a gobrāhmaṇahitārthāya deśasyāsya sukhāya ca
c tava caivāprameyasya vacanaṃ kartum udyataḥ
a evam uktvā dhanurmadhye baddhvā muṣṭim ariṃdamaḥ
c jyāśabdam akarot tīvraṃ diśaḥ śabdena pūrayan
a tena śabdena vitrastās tāṭakā vanavāsinaḥ
c tāṭakā ca susaṃkruddhā tena śabdena mohitā
a taṃ śabdam abhinidhyāya rākṣasī krodhamūrchitā
c śrutvā cābhyadravad vegād yataḥ śabdo viniḥsṛtaḥ
a tāṃ dṛṣṭvā rāghavaḥ kruddhāṃ vikṛtāṃ vikṛtānanām
c pramāṇenātivṛddhāṃ ca lakṣmaṇaṃ so 'bhyabhāṣata
a paśya lakṣmaṇa yakṣiṇyā bhairavaṃ dāruṇaṃ vapuḥ
c bhidyeran darśanād asyā bhīrūṇāṃ hṛdayāni ca
a enāṃ paśya durādharṣāṃ māyā balasamanvitām
c vinivṛttāṃ karomy adya hṛtakarṇāgranāsikām
a na hy enām utsahe hantuṃ strīsvabhāvena rakṣitām
c vīryaṃ cāsyā gatiṃ cāpi haniṣyāmīti me matiḥ
a evaṃ bruvāṇe rāme tu tāṭakā krodhamūrchitā
c udyamya bāhū garjantī rāmam evābhyadhāvata
a tām āpatantīṃ vegena vikrāntām aśanīm iva
c śareṇorasi vivyādha sā papāta mamāra ca
a tāṃ hatāṃ bhīmasaṃkāśāṃ dṛṣṭvā surapatis tadā
c sādhu sādhv iti kākutsthaṃ surāś ca samapūjayan
a uvāca paramaprītaḥ sahasrākṣaḥ puraṃdaraḥ
c surāś ca sarve saṃhṛṣṭā viśvāmitram athābruvan
a mune kauśike bhadraṃ te sendrāḥ sarve marudgaṇāḥ
c toṣitāḥ karmaṇānena snehaṃ darśaya rāghave
a prajāpater bhṛśāśvasya putrān satyaparākramān
c tapobalabhṛtān brahman rāghavāya nivedaya
a pātrabhūtaś ca te brahmaṃs tavānugamane dhṛtaḥ
c kartavyaṃ ca mahat karma surāṇāṃ rājasūnunā
a evam uktvā surāḥ sarve hṛṣṭā jagmur yathāgatam
c viśvāmitraṃ pūjayitvā tataḥ saṃdhyā pravartate
a tato munivaraḥ prītis tāṭakā vadhatoṣitaḥ
c mūrdhni rāmam upāghrāya idaṃ vacanam abravīt
a ihādya rajanīṃ rāma vasema śubhadarśana
c śvaḥ prabhāte gamiṣyāmas tad āśramapadaṃ mama
a atha tāṃ rajanīm uṣya viśvāmiro mahāyaśāḥ
c prahasya rāghavaṃ vākyam uvāca madhurākṣaram
a patituṣṭo 'smi bhadraṃ te rājaputra mahāyaśaḥ
c prītyā paramayā yukto dadāmy astrāṇi sarvaśaḥ
a devāsuragaṇān vāpi sagandharvoragān api
c yair amitrān prasahyājau vaśīkṛtya jayiṣyasi
a tāni divyāni bhadraṃ te dadāmy astrāṇi sarvaśaḥ
c daṇḍacakraṃ mahad divyaṃ tava dāsyāmi rāghava
a dharmacakraṃ tato vīra kālacakraṃ tathaiva ca
c viṣṇucakraṃ tathātyugram aindraṃ cakraṃ tathaiva ca
a vajram astraṃ naraśreṣṭha śaivaṃ śūlavaraṃ tathā
c astraṃ brahmaśiraś caiva aiṣīkam api rāghava
a dadāmi te mahābāho brāhmam astram anuttamam
c gade dve caiva kākutstha modakī śikharī ubhe
a pradīpte naraśārdūla prayacchāmi nṛpātmaja
c dharmapāśam ahaṃ rāma kālapāśaṃ tathaiva ca
a vāruṇaṃ pāśam astraṃ ca dadāny aham anuttamam
c aśanī dve prayacchāmi śuṣkārdre raghunandana
a dadāmi cāstraṃ painākam astraṃ nārāyaṇaṃ tathā
c āgneyam astra dayitaṃ śikharaṃ nāma nāmataḥ
a vāyavyaṃ prathamaṃ nāma dadāmi tava rāghava
c astraṃ hayaśiro nāma krauñcam astraṃ tathaiva ca
a śakti dvayaṃ ca kākutstha dadāmi tava cānagha
c kaṅkālaṃ musalaṃ ghoraṃ kāpālam atha kaṅkaṇam
a dhārayanty asurā yāni dadāmy etāni sarvaśaḥ
c vaidyādharaṃ mahāstraṃ ca nandanaṃ nāma nāmataḥ
a asiratnaṃ mahābāho dadāmi nṛvarātmaja
c gāndharvam astraṃ dayitaṃ mānavaṃ nāma nāmataḥ
a prasvāpanapraśamane dadmi sauraṃ ca rāghava
c darpaṇaṃ śoṣaṇaṃ caiva saṃtāpanavilāpane
a madanaṃ caiva durdharṣaṃ kandarpadayitaṃ tathā
c paiśācam astraṃ dayitaṃ mohanaṃ nāma nāmataḥ
e pratīccha naraśārdūla rājaputra mahāyaśaḥ
a tāmasaṃ naraśārdūla saumanaṃ ca mahābalam
c saṃvartaṃ caiva durdharṣaṃ mausalaṃ ca nṛpātmaja
a satyam astraṃ mahābāho tathā māyādharaṃ param
c ghoraṃ tejaḥprabhaṃ nāma paratejo'pakarṣaṇam
a somāstraṃ śiśiraṃ nāma tvāṣṭram astraṃ sudāmanam
c dāruṇaṃ ca bhagasyāpi śīteṣum atha mānavam
a etān nāma mahābāho kāmarūpān mahābalān
c gṛhāṇa paramodārān kṣipram eva nṛpātmaja
a sthitas tu prāṅmukho bhūtvā śucir nivaratas tadā
c dadau rāmāya suprīto mantragrāmam anuttamam
a japatas tu munes tasya viśvāmitrasya dhīmataḥ
c upatasthur mahārhāṇi sarvāṇy astrāṇi rāghavam
a ūcuś ca muditā rāmaṃ sarve prāñjalayas tadā
c ime sma paramodāra kiṃkarās tava rāghava
a pratigṛhya ca kākutsthaḥ samālabhya ca pāṇinā
c manasā me bhaviṣyadhvam iti tāny abhyacodayat
a tataḥ prītamanā rāmo viśvāmitraṃ mahāmunim
c abhivādya mahātejā gamanāyopacakrame
a pratigṛhya tato 'strāṇi prahṛṣṭavadanaḥ śuciḥ
c gacchann eva ca kākutstho viśvāmitram athābravīt
a gṛhītāstro 'smi bhagavan durādharṣaḥ surair api
c astrāṇāṃ tv aham icchāmi saṃhāraṃ munipuṃgava
a evaṃ bruvati kākutsthe viśvāmitro mahāmuniḥ
c saṃhāraṃ vyājahārātha dhṛtimān suvrataḥ śuciḥ
a satyavantaṃ satyakīrtiṃ dhṛṣṭaṃ rabhasam eva ca
c pratihārataraṃ nāma parāṅmukham avāṅmukham
a lakṣākṣaviṣamau caiva dṛḍhanābhasunābhakau
c daśākṣaśatavaktrau ca daśaśīrṣaśatodarau
a padmanābhamahānābhau dundunābhasunābhakau
c jyotiṣaṃ kṛśanaṃ caiva nairāśya vimalāv ubhau
a yaugandharaharidrau ca daityapramathanau tathā
c pitryaṃ saumanasaṃ caiva vidhūtamakarāv ubhau
a karavīrakaraṃ caiva dhanadhānyau ca rāghava
c kāmarūpaṃ kāmaruciṃ moham āvaraṇaṃ tathā
a jṛmbhakaṃ sarvanābhaṃ ca santānavaraṇau tathā
c bhṛśāśvatanayān rāma bhāsvarān kāmarūpiṇaḥ
a pratīccha mama bhadraṃ te pātrabhūto 'si rāghava
c divyabhāsvaradehāś ca mūrtimantaḥ sukhapradāḥ
a rāmaṃ prāñjalayo bhūtvābruvan madhurabhāṣiṇaḥ
c ime sma naraśārdūla śādhi kiṃ karavāma te
a gamyatām iti tān āha yatheṣṭaṃ raghunandanaḥ
c mānasāḥ kāryakāleṣu sāhāyyaṃ me kariṣyatha
a atha te rāmam āmantrya kṛtvā cāpi pradakṣiṇam
c evam astv iti kākutstham uktvā jagmur yathāgatam
a sa ca tān rāghavo jñātvā viśvāmitraṃ mahāmunim
c gacchann evātha madhuraṃ ślakṣṇaṃ vacanam abravīt
a kiṃ nv etan meghasaṃkāśaṃ parvatasyāvidūrataḥ
c vṛkṣaṣaṇḍam ito bhāti paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hi me
a darśanīyaṃ mṛgākīrṇaṃ manoharam atīva ca
c nānāprakāraiḥ śakunair valgubhāṣair alaṃkṛtam
a niḥsṛtāḥ sma muniśreṣṭha kāntārād romaharṣaṇāt
c anayā tv avagacchāmi deśasya sukhavattayā
a sarvaṃ me śaṃsa bhagavan kasyāśramapadaṃ tv idam
c saṃprāptā yatra te pāpā brahmaghnā duṣṭacāriṇaḥ
a atha tasyāprameyasya tad vanaṃ paripṛcchataḥ
c viśvāmitro mahātejā vyākhyātum upacakrame
a eṣa pūrvāśramo rāma vāmanasya mahātmanaḥ
c siddhāśrama iti khyātaḥ siddho hy atra mahātapāḥ
a etasminn eva kāle tu rājā vairocanir baliḥ
c nirjitya daivatagaṇān sendrāṃś ca samarudgaṇān
e kārayām āsa tad rājyaṃ triṣu lokeṣu viśrutaḥ
a bales tu yajamānasya devāḥ sāgnipurogamāḥ
c samāgamya svayaṃ caiva viṣṇum ūcur ihāśrame
a balir vairocanir viṣṇo yajate yajñam uttamam
c asamāpte kratau tasmin svakāryam abhipadyatām
a ye cainam abhivartante yācitāra itas tataḥ
c yac ca yatra yathāvac ca sarvaṃ tebhyaḥ prayacchati
a sa tvaṃ surahitārthāya māyāyogam upāśritaḥ
c vāmanatvaṃ gato viṣṇo kuru kalyāṇam uttamam
a ayaṃ siddhāśramo nāma prasādāt te bhaviṣyati
c siddhe karmaṇi deveśa uttiṣṭha bhagavann itaḥ
a atha viṣṇur mahātejā adityāṃ samajāyata
c vāmanaṃ rūpam āsthāya vairocanim upāgamat
a trīn kramān atha bhikṣitvā pratigṛhya ca mānataḥ
c ākramya lokāṃl lokātmā sarvabhūtahite rataḥ
a mahendrāya punaḥ prādān niyamya balim ojasā
c trailokyaṃ sa mahātejāś cakre śakravaśaṃ punaḥ
a tenaiṣa pūrvam ākrānta āśramaḥ śramanāśanaḥ
c mayāpi bhaktyā tasyaiṣa vāmanasyopabhujyate
a etam āśramam āyānti rākṣasā vighnakāriṇaḥ
c atra te puruṣavyāghra hantavyā duṣṭacāriṇaḥ
a adya gacchāmahe rāma siddhāśramam anuttamam
c tad āśramapadaṃ tāta tavāpy etad yathā mama
a taṃ dṛṣṭvā munayaḥ sarve siddhāśramanivāsinaḥ
c utpatyotpatya sahasā viśvāmitram apūjayan
a yathārhaṃ cakrire pūjāṃ viśvāmitrāya dhīmate
c tathaiva rājaputrābhyām akurvann atithikriyām
a muhūrtam atha viśrāntau rājaputrāv ariṃdamau
c prāñjalī muniśārdūlam ūcatū raghunandanau
a adyaiva dīkṣāṃ praviśa bhadraṃ te munipuṃgava
c siddhāśramo 'yaṃ siddhaḥ syāt satyam astu vacas tava
a evam ukto mahātejā viśvāmitro mahāmuniḥ
c praviveśa tadā dīkṣāṃ niyato niyatendriyaḥ
a kumārāv api tāṃ rātrim uṣitvā susamāhitau
c prabhātakāle cotthāya viśvāmitram avandatām
a atha tau deśakālajñau rājaputrāv ariṃdamau
c deśe kāle ca vākyajñāv abrūtāṃ kauśikaṃ vacaḥ
a bhagavañ śrotum icchāvo yasmin kāle niśācarau
c saṃrakṣaṇīyau tau brahman nātivarteta tatkṣaṇam
a evaṃ bruvāṇau kākutsthau tvaramāṇau yuyutsayā
c sarve te munayaḥ prītāḥ praśaśaṃsur nṛpātmajau
a adya prabhṛti ṣaḍrātraṃ rakṣataṃ rāghavau yuvām
c dīkṣāṃ gato hy eṣa munir maunitvaṃ ca gamiṣyati
a tau tu tad vacanaṃ śrutvā rājaputrau yaśasvinau
c anidrau ṣaḍahorātraṃ tapovanam arakṣatām
a upāsāṃ cakratur vīrau yattau paramadhanvinau
c rarakṣatur munivaraṃ viśvāmitram ariṃdamau
a atha kāle gate tasmin ṣaṣṭhe 'hani samāgate
c saumitram abravīd rāmo yatto bhava samāhitaḥ
a rāmasyaivaṃ bruvāṇasya tvaritasya yuyutsayā
c prajajvāla tato vediḥ sopādhyāyapurohitā
a mantravac ca yathānyāyaṃ yajño 'sau saṃpravartate
c ākāśe ca mahāñ śabdaḥ prādur āsīd bhayānakaḥ
a āvārya gaganaṃ megho yathā prāvṛṣi nirgataḥ
c tathā māyāṃ vikurvāṇau rākṣasāv abhyadhāvatām
a mārīcaś ca subāhuś ca tayor anucarās tathā
c āgamya bhīmasaṃkāśā rudhiraughān avāsṛjan
a tāv āpatantau sahasā dṛṣṭvā rājīvalocanaḥ
c lakṣmaṇaṃ tv abhisaṃprekṣya rāmo vacanam abravīt
a paśya lakṣmaṇa durvṛttān rākṣasān piśitāśanān
c mānavāstrasamādhūtān anilena yathāghanān
a mānavaṃ paramodāram astraṃ paramabhāsvaram
c cikṣepa paramakruddho mārīcor asi rāghavaḥ
a sa tena paramāstreṇa mānavena samāhitaḥ
c saṃpūrṇaṃ yojanaśataṃ kṣiptaḥ sāgarasaṃplave
a vicetanaṃ vighūrṇantaṃ śīteṣubalapīḍitam
c nirastaṃ dṛśya mārīcaṃ rāmo lakṣmaṇam abravīt
a paśya lakṣmaṇa śīteṣuṃ mānavaṃ dharmasaṃhitam
c mohayitvā nayaty enaṃ na ca prāṇair viyujyate
a imān api vadhiṣyāmi nirghṛṇān duṣṭacāriṇaḥ
c rākṣasān pāpakarmasthān yajñaghnān rudhirāśanān
a vigṛhya sumahac cāstram āgneyaṃ raghunandanaḥ
c subāhur asi cikṣepa sa viddhaḥ prāpatad bhuvi
a śeṣān vāyavyam ādāya nijaghāna mahāyaśāḥ
c rāghavaḥ paramodāro munīnāṃ mudam āvahan
a sa hatvā rākṣasān sarvān yajñaghnān raghunandanaḥ
c ṛṣibhiḥ pūjitas tatra yathendro vijaye purā
a atha yajñe samāpte tu viśvāmitro mahāmuniḥ
c nirītikā diśo dṛṣṭvā kākutstham idam abravīt
a kṛtārtho 'smi mahābāho kṛtaṃ guruvacas tvayā
c siddhāśramam idaṃ satyaṃ kṛtaṃ rāma mahāyaśaḥ
a atha tāṃ rajanīṃ tatra kṛtārthau rāmalakṣaṇau
c ūṣatur muditau vīrau prahṛṣṭenāntarātmanā
a prabhātāyāṃ tu śarvaryāṃ kṛtapaurvāhṇikakriyau
c viśvāmitram ṛṣīṃś cānyān sahitāv abhijagmatuḥ
a abhivādya muniśreṣṭhaṃ jvalantam iva pāvakam
c ūcatur madhurodāraṃ vākyaṃ madhurabhāṣiṇau
a imau svo muniśārdūla kiṃkarau samupasthitau
c ājñāpaya yatheṣṭaṃ vai śāsanaṃ karavāva kim
a evam ukte tatas tābhyāṃ sarva eva maharṣayaḥ
c viśvāmitraṃ puraskṛtya rāmaṃ vacanam abruvan
a maithilasya naraśreṣṭha janakasya bhaviṣyati
c yajñaḥ paramadharmiṣṭhas tatra yāsyāmahe vayam
a tvaṃ caiva naraśārdūla sahāsmābhir gamiṣyasi
c adbhutaṃ ca dhanūratnaṃ tatra tvaṃ draṣṭum arhasi
a tad dhi pūrvaṃ naraśreṣṭha dattaṃ sadasi daivataiḥ
c aprameyabalaṃ ghoraṃ makhe paramabhāsvaram
a nāsya devā na gandharvā nāsurā na ca rākṣasāḥ
c kartum āropaṇaṃ śaktā na kathaṃ cana mānuṣāḥ
a dhanuṣas tasya vīryaṃ hi jijñāsanto mahīkṣitaḥ
c na śekur āropayituṃ rājaputrā mahābalāḥ
a tad dhanur naraśārdūla maithilasya mahātmanaḥ
c tatra drakṣyasi kākutstha yajñaṃ cādbhutadarśanam
a tad dhi yajñaphalaṃ tena maithilenottamaṃ dhanuḥ
c yācitaṃ naraśārdūla sunābhaṃ sarvadaivataiḥ
a evam uktvā munivaraḥ prasthānam akarot tadā
c sarṣisaṃghaḥ sakākutstha āmantrya vanadevatāḥ
a svasti vo 'stu gamiṣyāmi siddhaḥ siddhāśramād aham
c uttare jāhnavītīre himavantaṃ śiloccayam
a pradakṣiṇaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā siddhāśramam anuttamam
c uttarāṃ diśam uddiśya prasthātum upacakrame
a taṃ vrajantaṃ munivaram anvagād anusāriṇām
c śakaṭī śatamātraṃ tu prayāṇe brahmavādinām
a mṛgapakṣigaṇāś caiva siddhāśramanivāsinaḥ
c anujagmur mahātmānaṃ viśvāmitraṃ mahāmunim
a te gatvā dūram adhvānaṃ lambamāne divākare
c vāsaṃ cakrur munigaṇāḥ śoṇākūle samāhitāḥ
a te 'staṃ gate dinakare snātvā hutahutāśanāḥ
c viśvāmitraṃ puraskṛtya niṣedur amitaujasaḥ
a rāmo 'pi sahasaumitrir munīṃs tān abhipūjya ca
c agrato niṣasādātha viśvāmitrasya dhīmataḥ
a atha rāmo mahātejā viśvāmitraṃ mahāmunim
c papraccha muniśārdūlaṃ kautūhalasamanvitaḥ
a bhagavan ko nv ayaṃ deśaḥ samṛddhavanaśobhitaḥ
c śrotum icchāmi bhadraṃ te vaktum arhasi tattvataḥ
a codito rāmavākyena kathayām āsa suvrataḥ
c tasya deśasya nikhilam ṛṣimadhye mahātapāḥ
a brahmayonir mahān āsīt kuśo nāma mahātapāḥ
c vaidarbhyāṃ janayām āsa caturaḥ sadṛśān sutān
a kuśāmbaṃ kuśanābhaṃ ca ādhūrta rajasaṃ vasum
c dīptiyuktān mahotsāhān kṣatradharmacikīrṣayā
e tān uvāca kuśaḥ putrān dharmiṣṭhān satyavādinaḥ
a kuśasya vacanaṃ śrutvā catvāro lokasaṃmatāḥ
c niveśaṃ cakrire sarve purāṇāṃ nṛvarās tadā
a kuśāmbas tu mahātejāḥ kauśāmbīm akarot purīm
c kuśanābhas tu dharmātmā paraṃ cakre mahodayam
a ādhūrtarajaso rāma dharmāraṇyaṃ mahīpatiḥ
c cakre puravaraṃ rājā vasuś cakre girivrajam
a eṣā vasumatī rāma vasos tasya mahātmanaḥ
c ete śailavarāḥ pañca prakāśante samantataḥ
a sumāgadhī nadī ramyā māgadhān viśrutāyayau
c pañcānāṃ śailamukhyānāṃ madhye māleva śobhate
a saiṣā hi māgadhī rāma vasos tasya mahātmanaḥ
c pūrvābhicaritā rāma sukṣetrā sasyamālinī
a kuśanābhas tu rājarṣiḥ kanyāśatam anuttamam
c janayām āsa dharmātmā ghṛtācyāṃ raghunandana
a tās tu yauvanaśālinyo rūpavatyaḥ svalaṃkṛtāḥ
c udyānabhūmim āgamya prāvṛṣīva śatahradāḥ
a gāyantyo nṛtyamānāś ca vādayantyaś ca rāghava
c āmodaṃ paramaṃ jagmur varābharaṇabhūṣitāḥ
a atha tāś cārusarvāṅgyo rūpeṇāpratimā bhuvi
c udyānabhūmim āgamya tārā iva ghanāntare
a tāḥ sarvaguṇasaṃpannā rūpayauvanasaṃyutāḥ
c dṛṣṭvā sarvātmako vāyur idaṃ vacanam abravīt
